Yellow River's Flood May Divert into the Grand Canal and Enter the Huai River 68

Han Fuju Requests the Central Government to Prepare Urgent Disaster Relief and Sends Telegrams to Hebei and Henan Requesting the Blocking of Breaches Along the Banks

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Yellow River floods in Hebei and Henan provinces invaded Shandong province, the areas affected by the overflow have become flooded lands. The Shandong Provincial Government and the River Affairs Bureau have been urgently reporting the disaster situation from various counties and the Caozhou Eight Counties River Works Promotion Association for days, which is extremely pitiful. In addition, continuous heavy rain in Heze County, pouring down all night, caused the water level in the rivers northwest of the city to rise sharply. Newly built dams were breaching successively, and fields were being flooded. The current is vast and the source is strong, causing a dangerous flood. If rescue measures are not taken quickly, once the southern bank breaches, there will be a risk of severing the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai railways, diverting the Grand Canal, and entering the Huai River. The disaster situation is extremely serious, unprecedented in decades. Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju, in addition to sending telegrams to the disaster-stricken county magistrates to cooperate with the people to desperately defend and rescue, has also been sending telegrams to Chairman Chiang, Chairman Lin, President Wang, Minister Huang, and the Relief Committee for days, requesting that they quickly prepare for blocking the breaches and quickly release urgent relief to save lives. He also sent telegrams to the chairmen Liu of Hebei and Henan, requesting that they quickly take measures to block the breaches along the banks and prevent the floods from spreading, so as not to expand the disaster. The various telegrams are recorded below.

Telegrams to the Government 69

㈠ Urgent, must arrive immediately, addressed to Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, Minister Huang of the Ministry of Interior, and Chairman Chiang of Guling: According to successive telegrams from the Heze County Government, the south bank of the Yellow River in Erfenzhuang, Dongming County, Hebei Province, breached at Zhenri, the water level is more than one zhang high, heading straight for western Shandong; also, the south bank of the Yellow River in Yuanzhai, Kaocheng County, Henan Province, breached at Zhen evening, flooding Kaocheng and the Shandong counties of Shan, Jun, and Cao; also, the north bank above Shitou Village, Section 1 of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, has a breach several li wide, flooding Changyuan, Hua County, Puyang, and the Shandong counties of Pu, Fan, and Shouyang. The south bank of the Yellow River in Hebei and Henan provinces has always had many dangerous projects. Once a breach occurs, not only will dozens of counties in western Shandong be flooded, but there will be a risk of severing the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai railways, diverting the Grand Canal, and entering the Huai River. In addition to ordering the disaster-stricken counties to desperately defend and rescue, I am hereby reporting this for your information, and requesting that you instruct the preparation of blocking the breaches and the release of urgent relief to save lives. Please also issue instructions for me to follow. Han Fuju respectfully bows. ㈡ (Title omitted) The situation of the Yellow River flooding and inundating Shandong Province has been reported in detail. Recently, Sun Zerang, the magistrate of Heze County, reported in an urgent telegram that there was heavy rain all night, and all the newly built embankments overflowed. The water has now reached the city wall, with a depth of three or four chi on flat ground. The northwest of the city has become a flooded land, and fields have been submerged. The Taoyuanji area in the southwest is also being flooded from Kaocheng, and the disaster situation is severe. Many people have drowned and have no food or clothing. Please allocate funds for urgent relief. Gu Liangyou, the commander of the Caozhou militia, also sent a telegram with the same information, and ordered officers and soldiers of the militia to do their best to protect. In addition, Wei Hanzhang, the magistrate of Cao County, telegraphed that villages within ten li to the west, south, and north of the county seat are mostly surrounded by water, with a local depth of three to five chi. He has ordered all districts to take measures to block the breaches and repair the city wall day and night. In addition, Liu Jing, the magistrate of Dingtao County, telegraphed that the heavy rain at night caused the water to rise continuously, and the embankments collapsed as soon as they were blocked. All the villages in the south of the county have been flooded. In addition, Wang Xizhen, the magistrate of Shan County, telegraphed that the breach in the Yellow River in Henan Province has reached the Laojun Ditch, the border between Cao and Shan counties, with a depth of about one zhang and five chi. He has ordered his subordinates to assess the situation and take measures to defend. In addition to telegraphed orders to desperately defend and rescue the victims, and reporting separately, I am hereby reporting this. Your official, Han Fuju, respectfully bows. ㈢ (Title omitted) I have reported in detail on the situation of the breaches in the Yellow River in Henan and Hebei provinces and their inundation of Shandong Province in telegrams. In addition, I have reported that the Heze County Government and the Caozhou Eight Counties River Works Promotion Association successively reported in their telegrams that there was heavy rain all day, pouring down all night, causing the water level in the rivers northwest of the city to rise sharply, and the newly built embankments collapsed successively, and the fields were almost completely flooded. The four Qian Rivers in the west were all filled with water from the Yellow River, overflowing the embankments, flowing to the northwest, and merging with Weizhuang in the east, penetrating the entire northern territory and heading east towards Juye. The current is very strong and is still rising. The water situation in Cao County is even more vast. The continuous flood and overflow has turned all the counties in western Shandong into a muddy country and continues to increase, what a dangerous situation. In addition to ordering the disaster-stricken counties to desperately defend and rescue, and dispatching special personnel to supervise the work, I am hereby reporting this and requesting approval, ordering the preparation of blocking the breaches and the rapid implementation of relief to save lives. Please also issue instructions for me to follow. Your official, Han Fuju, respectfully bows.

Telegram to the Relief Committee 70

(1) Urgent Arrival Required, Nanjing.

Respected Relief Committee,

Regarding the situations in Henan and Hebei provinces where the Yellow River breached its banks, flooding areas in Shandong province, a telegram has already been sent to you. Now, according to subsequent telegrams from the Heze County government and the Cao Prefecture Eight-County River Works Promotion Association, torrential rain has been falling like pouring water on cold days, ceaselessly throughout the night. The river currents to the northwest of the city have swelled violently, and newly built dikes have successively collapsed, inundating almost all the fields and crops. The four western dry riverbeds are all filled with Yellow River water, overflowing the embankments and flowing to Weizhuang in the northwest, converging eastward, traversing the entire northern territory, and heading towards Juye. The source of the water flow is currently very strong and is still increasing. Furthermore, the situation in Cao County is particularly severe. Given the continuous flooding in recent days, the counties in western Shandong have all become a watery realm, and the situation continues to worsen, posing a significant danger. In addition to telegraphing the central government to urgently plan for repairs, we are specifically telegraphing your esteemed committee to quickly organize and provide emergency relief to save lives. We await your prompt instructions on how to proceed.

Respectfully,

Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government.

Yellow River Water Reaches Jiangsu Province 72

Zhouzhai in Dangshan County Already Submerged

Water Speed is Seventy Li Per Day

Transportation Bureau Ordered by Provincial Government to Defend

Yangzhou Correspondence: The Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau has received a telegram from the Provincial Government stating that Fengxian County reports that the Yellow River water has already reached Dazhai in Dangshan. In addition to the two thousand workers supervised by the bureau to reinforce and block the breaches in the old Yellow River embankment at Zhouzhai and Gaozhai in Dangshan Prefecture, a telegram should also be sent to Pei County to fully cooperate in blocking Gaozhai, while Dangshan County should fully defend Zhouzhai. Another telegram from the county on [a certain date] states that the Yellow River water has reached Zhouzhai, with a waterhead one li wide and five chi deep, and a rear flow five li wide and more than one zhang deep. The water speed is approximately seventy li per day. The bureau is currently supervising workers to block the Gaozhai dike opening and requests that Pei County expedite its arrival. Considering that the Yellow River water has reached Zhouzhai in Dangshan County, it may flow north into Zhaoyang and then into Weishan Lake, or southeast along the old course of the Yellow River. It is estimated that it will enter the canal within two or three days. The central canal should first establish defenses, assigning specific responsibilities. Meanwhile, efforts should continue day and night to gather laborers for defense and to intensify inspections, without the slightest negligence or delay. This matter should be strictly observed and reported. In times of urgent defense needs, the county magistrates of each county should listen to the commands of the Transportation Bureau to unify authority and avoid disputes. Furthermore, the Transportation Bureau has already telegraphed the Huaipiao Department of the Engineering Office to establish defenses and conduct patrols starting immediately, and to dispatch staff to Hanzhuang and Weishan Lake to patrol and report the water situation regularly. It is also heard that the Transportation Bureau plans to gather laborers immediately to block key points such as Lanjia Dam and Weishan Lake to strengthen defenses (August 17).

Restoration of Pinghan Railway Transportation 73

Express Trains Running, Regular Trains Terminate on Both Banks

Yellow River Bridge Tilting, Repair Project Enormous

Railway Bureau Losses Approximately 500,000 Yuan in One Week

Hankou Correspondence: The Pinghan Railway was affected by the Yellow River's rise, causing the railway bridge to tilt and the tracks to be damaged. Trains could not pass directly. From the 9th to the 15th, north-south transportation was cut off for a week. The Railway Bureau's business losses, estimated at 60,000 yuan per day, totaled 420,000 yuan, plus other losses, for a total of approximately 500,000 yuan. Now that the water level is gradually receding, the special express train conducted a trial crossing of the bridge on the 16th, and full line operation was restored on the 17th. However, the bridge construction is a major undertaking, and it will be difficult to repair it in a short time. To avoid increasing the danger, all regular trains will temporarily terminate on both banks. The Railway Bureau's news is recorded as follows:

Inspection of Bridge Conditions 74

The Pinghan Railway Management Committee, previously received a report from the Zhengzhou Station Master that the Yellow River had risen and flooded the railway bridge. It specifically dispatched the Chief of the Engineering Department, Wang Jinzhi, to rush to the site for inspection. Mr. Wang telegraphed the Committee on the 15th, stating, "The situation of the Yellow River bridge was quite serious in the previous few days. After rescue efforts day and night by this office, it has slightly eased by the 15th. All southbound locomotives can reach Bridge No. 50, and northbound locomotives can reach Bridge No. 90. However, the section from Bridge No. 50 to Bridge No. 90 is definitely impassable for locomotives. To facilitate transportation, it is decided that from the 16th onwards, the first and second trains will use the lightest 20-ton or 15-ton Pingdong vehicle for northbound and southbound transfer. However, the section from Bridge No. 50 to Bridge No. 90 must be pushed by manpower. The transfer time is limited to 17:30 to 20:00 (5 PM to 8 PM) daily. Please do not delay, so as not to hinder the bridge work," and so on.

Temporary Ferrying Measures 75

The Committee also received a telegram from the Second Section Chief of Zhengzhou, agreeing on temporary ferrying measures, which stated, in brief, that regarding the issue of train traffic on the Yellow River Bridge, a settlement has been reached with the construction party. It is decided that starting on the 16th, the first and second express trains will be transferred first. The method is that the construction party is concerned that the original trains are too heavy to cross the bridge and may cause danger. It is agreed that six third-class cars, converted from 20-ton covered cars, will be prepared on the north and south banks to transfer passengers, postal and baggage cars. They will still be pushed across the bridge tracks by manpower. The transfer time is set from 11 AM to 2 PM to avoid hindering the work. Zhengzhou Station is instructed to prepare forty laborers, divided between the north and south banks, to be responsible for transferring luggage and pushing cars. To maintain order, the police have been consulted and capable police officers have been dispatched. The train department has also dispatched the Deputy Section Chief of Zhengzhou and the Deputy Section Chief of Xinxiang to supervise the car service inspectors and station staff to jointly assist in directing and maintaining order. To adapt to the transfer time, the departure times of the first and second trains should be changed to avoid hindering the construction party's work.

Advance Departure Times 76

The Committee, after receiving

the telegram, immediately

instructed the Car Service Department to formulate the following measures for advancing the departure times of the express trains: (1) The first train will depart from Qianmen, Beiping at 15:30 (3:30 PM), arrive at the north bank of the Yellow River at 11:30 AM the next day, depart the south bank of the Yellow River at 14:35, and arrive at Dazhimen, Hankou at 9:30 AM on the third day. (2) The second train will depart from Dazhimen, Hankou at 16:00 (4:00 PM), arrive at the south bank of the Yellow River at 10:57 AM the next day, depart the north bank of the Yellow River at 15:40, and arrive in Beiping at 10:58 AM on the third day. As for the regular express trains in both directions, they will all go to both banks of the Yellow River. All passengers and luggage will be pushed across the bridge in the above-mentioned covered cars. When the special express trains cross the bridge, because they must be pushed by manpower, the journey will take 42 hours, three hours slower than usual.

Department Consultation on Repairs 77

The Pinghan Railway Management Committee is paying close attention to this obstruction of the Yellow River. In addition to sending the Chief of the Engineering Department, Wang Jinzhi, to the site for inspection, the Chairman of the Committee, He Jingwu, and the Committee Member, Xiao Qizhan, have also departed successively to supervise the repair work. The tracks at Zhan Dian on the north bank were repaired earlier, and special trains could barely pass. However, six or seventy holes in the middle of the bridge are half-filled with mud and half-tilted by about two inches due to water damage. The repair project is huge, and the cost is considerable. How to carry out the construction requires careful planning. Now, the Ministry of Railways has dispatched Wu Qiyou, a designing engineer from the Jinpu Railway, to Zhengzhou via the Longhai Railway to consult with the Chairman of the Committee, He Jingwu, the Committee Member, Xiao Qizhan, and the Chief of the Engineering Department, Wang Jinzhi, on repair methods. The plan will be submitted to the Ministry for approval soon and implemented. The Yellow River Railway Bridge has long exceeded its insurance period, and with the riverbed rising daily, there is a constant risk of being washed away. If it is not thoroughly repaired, the vast natural barrier will forever be a fearsome route for travelers (17th).

Two-Day Tour of Scenic Spots in Jinan

Jinan Correspondence: After Feng Yuxiang arrived in Jinan on the 15th, he, accompanied by Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, toured Thousand Buddha Mountain and visited the swimming pool at 6 AM on the 16th. Li Xin, Zhang Jiyong, and others also followed Feng. At 3:10 PM, they left Jinan heading south. The engine-hauled cars traveled very fast, arriving in Tai'an at 4:45 PM. Tai'an County Magistrate Zhou Baihuang and representatives from various agencies, as well as Feng's guards who had arrived in Tai'an earlier, all welcomed him at the station. Inspection Report of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei 79

Qingjiang, a City Twice Captured by the Red Bandits

Qingjiang Correspondence: Since the Red Bandits attempted to cross the Gan River westward and invade Jishui and Xingan, the Gan-Yue line has been blocked for nearly a month. The 14th Army has been ordered to restore traffic on the Gan River, stationing troops along the river. Ships can gradually travel up and down, but when passing through certain dangerous sections between Xingan and Xiajiang, they are still often at risk of being shot at by bandit troops. Sometimes only the ship's cabin is damaged, and sometimes passengers are killed. The reporter waited quietly for three days but did not see a single ship safely sailing from the upper river. Therefore, he abandoned the inspection of the Gan-Yue line and instead embarked on a trip to western Jiangxi, sailing up the Yuan River. After traveling about ten li upstream, he saw three or four wooden planks floating on the water, with faint traces of writing. He picked one up and saw the words "Strive for all Soviet areas, fight as one." The boatman caught sight of it, snatched it, and threw it into the river, saying, "Lao Yuan (meaning a common address for a fellow townsman from another province, like 'brother' or 'sir'), did you pick up this plank in the river? Two or three months ago, my brother was traveling from Xinyu to Zhangshu by boat when the water was high. There were many such wooden planks floating down. He picked up several pieces to use as firewood, but the water police gave him trouble." He was also asked if the harvest was good. Then they went to rest in the temple. Zhang Jiyong, Li Qi, and others stayed at the foot of the mountain, while Feng himself stayed at the Five Worthies Temple. According to news here, Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, will arrive in Tai'an tomorrow to meet with Feng. Also, while Feng was traveling, someone led a child to kneel and welcome him by the roadside. It is said that they were father and son, extremely poor and pitiful. Last year, when Feng was in Tai'an, he gave them money for clothes and found them a bowl of rice to eat, so they came to kneel and welcome him (17th).

Guangdong Province

Levy of National Defense Donation 80

Taxing Merchants at 2% of Capital

Collected by Public Security Bureaus Starting from the 15th

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangzhou community recently organized a Public Air Defense Committee, formulated measures, and raised funds to purchase aircraft to consolidate air defenses. The method of raising funds is to hold a national defense donation, soliciting donations from all stores in the city. The donation standard is to levy 2% of the store's business license and business tax amount. Chen Jitang instructed the Provincial Public Security Bureau to be responsible for handling the matter. After receiving the order, the Public Security Bureau specifically sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday to request a copy of the city's store business licenses and business tax amounts in its possession to levy the tax according to the amount, and decided to start collecting it today (15th). The collection measures are as follows: (1) The donation will be paid at 2% of the amount on the business license. (2) If a store has not obtained a business license due to small business operations, it should be exempt from paying this national defense donation. (3) The business license amount should be the standard for collecting donations. (4) Long strips with the words "National Defense Donation Received for Business License Amount" will be created and issued. Stores that have paid the donation will affix the printed strips to the front of their doors for verification. (5) Donation tickets will be in quadruplicate. One copy will be given to the store for receipt, two copies will be submitted to the Public Security Bureau for storage and transfer, and one copy will be stored in the Public Security Bureau for future reference, with the bureau's seal affixed as a guarantee. (6) The national defense donation will be checked and collected by staff assigned by each Public Security Bureau to go to each store, and there must be no errors. (7) The director of each Public Security Bureau will be fully responsible for this donation. (8) The collection of donations will be handled concurrently by the police donation collectors of each Public Security Bureau. (9) The donation collection will begin on August 15th and must be completed within one month (August 15th).

Special Correspondent of this Newspaper: Ren An 81

Discovered, and Charged with Communicating with Bandits

"Later, although he was guaranteed by the Shipping Guild and narrowly escaped death, the disaster of imprisonment has not yet been lifted." Upon hearing this, the reporter thanked him for his kindness and asked why his sailcloth was so tattered that it only had a slight effect on harnessing the wind. He sighed and said, "We don't have enough to eat, how can we have extra money for anything else? In these times, soldiers and taxes are frequent. Many boatmen have abandoned their boats and are hiding deep in their homes. Those who cannot leave and are working are forced to do so by hunger." As they were talking, suddenly the yellow dust obscured the sun in the left front, and the waves gradually increased. The boatman quickly reeled in the cable and turned the rudder, just barely making it to the right bank when a violent wind roared in, followed by heavy rain and huge waves, causing the boat to capsize and tilt greatly. Those sitting upright in the cabin could not even lie flat. This lasted for about two hours before the wind died down and the river became calm. Several boats carrying garlic were broken by the wind and waves, and garlic floated in the river, which the fishermen eagerly collected. Upon arriving in Qingjiang, the soldiers guarding the city were just closing the city gates, as the sun had already set in the west.

The entire territory of Qingjiang covers approximately 3,800 square li, with a population of approximately 230,000. The main product is rice, with more than enough for local consumption, and about 200,000 shi are sold to other places annually. Special products include about 30,000 shi of melon seeds, priced at about 15 yuan per shi, and about 10,000 shi of tangerines, priced at about 5 yuan per shi (other details are in the Zhangshuzhen correspondence). However, since the bandits became rampant, many villages have been taken over by bandits. In 1919, the bandits captured the city twice, looting, killing, and setting fires, causing great damage. The biggest loss was the destruction of the Datong Public Pawnshop. The pawnshop (i.e., public pawnshop) had a long history and considerable capital. Every year, it used its profits to carry out a wide range of charitable activities. The manager, Mr. Zhou, was a wealthy gentleman who had been transporting cash to his home in advance. When the bandits arrived, he fled to Nanchang. Because there was no cash in the pawnshop, no one tried to find a way to take charge and negotiate, so the bandits unconditionally returned all pawned items worth less than three yuan to their original owners, and collected principal and interest on items worth more than three yuan. Valuables were confiscated. Later, Mr. Zhou returned to his hometown and vehemently denied having public funds at his home, which aroused public anger. He then conspired with the county magistrate to lure and kill him with wine. In addition, merchants' inventories, such as oil, salt, and rice, were forcibly sold by the bandits for only two cents per yuan. Fortunately, most of the office workers and wealthy residents had fled, and only three people were killed. However, there were many cases of kidnapping for ransom.

The kidnapping and ransom business is currently flourishing. The county government recently seized a sample of a bandit kidnapping and intimidation letter, which is copied as follows: "Mr. So-and-so, Greetings. Our army is struggling to overthrow imperialism, overthrow the rule of a certain party, eliminate feudal forces, carry out land revolution, and seek national independence for China and the liberation of the working, peasant, and laboring masses of the whole country. In order to complete the above great task, we urgently need huge military and political funds. We have long admired your abundant savings and generosity. Therefore, we are sending you a letter in advance, asking you to donate a certain amount of military pay in silver and pay it in full within a few days. We will issue a receipt (protection), and then protect your life and property. We trust that this small amount will not be refused in any way. Greetings, Team Leader So-and-so, Political Commissar So-and-so."

Songjiang

Store Owner Missing, Declared Liquidation 82

Yue Temple Street is a prosperous commercial area. However, this year, due to the low price of rice, all industries have been depressed. All major stores have shown poor business, but Tongfengtai Foreign Goods Store, due to the store owner Shen Changshou's good management, has had very developed business. Unexpectedly, on the 20th of this month, the store owner took money to Shanghai to pay bills. Before leaving, he told his family that he would go to his relative Chen Youquan's house in Rinanqiao via Shanghai and stay for about two or three days. The next day, wholesalers in Shanghai sent someone to Songjiang to collect the money. The store was already very surprised. Then the Chen family in Rinanqiao also waited for Shen to arrive and sent someone to Songjiang to urge him. Then the family became alarmed and realized that Shen Changshou was missing. They hired people to go to Shanghai to search and inquire, but found no news. It has been more than a week now, and the store has stopped business. His wife, Shen Shi, hired lawyer Zhang Zhijie to declare liquidation. According to rumors, Shen Changshou looked honest, so he absorbed a large amount of deposits from various households. The suspension of business and liquidation must be due to financial turnover problems, so he came up with this strategy. One saying is that Shen owes more than 10,000 gold, but he has only been married to Ms. Shi for four months, so the family is crying day and night, and the situation is tragic.

Autumn Silkworm Market News in Rural Areas 83

This year's autumn silkworms are twice as many as in the past. A week ago, due to the drought and lack of rain, the mulberry leaves were withered and yellow. Most farmers were deeply worried. Currently, there are occasional thunderstorms, and silkworm and farmland have benefited greatly. Currently, the autumn silkworms in Yeqiao, Shitangwan, Bashiqiao, Hujiadu, Dongting, Zhouxin Town, Daqiangmen, Chang'anqiao, Zhangjingqiao, Dangkou, and other areas are mostly in the second and third sleep stages. Zhangcun, Nanqiao, Rongxiang, Yangjingyuan, Hudai, Jiangxiqiao, Anzhen, Outangqiao, Qianzhou, Yuqi, Lishe, Beiqi'fang, Fuzhou Village, and other places are in the early sleep stages. The silkworms are in good condition. The market price of mulberry leaves is between 3.50 yuan and 2.00 yuan per load. If the weather does not change drastically, the future harvest will be good. This is also good news for the future of silk.

Tax Dispute in the Tobacco Industry Unresolved 84

Zhu Qi, the newly appointed Director of the License Tax Collection Office in this county, plans to double the license tax for the tobacco industry in this county, which has aroused repercussions in the industry. He sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to forward to the Collection Office to strive to maintain the original amount. After receiving the letter, the office still insisted on its opinion, stating that the license tax for tobacco and alcohol is related to both the Ministry and Provincial treasury and is listed as a legitimate income. Last year's selection committee may have had some inconsistencies in the tax rates for the merchants, which should be corrected according to regulations. It immediately replied to the County Chamber of Commerce, forwarding the letter to the industry to persuade them to comply with regulations, pay taxes, obtain licenses, and not provide any excuse for obstruction, and so on. After receiving the letter, the industry still expressed dissatisfaction. Yesterday, it specifically issued an emergency notice to all members of the industry, ordering them to convene a general meeting of members at the association on the afternoon of the 19th to discuss solutions.

Yang Lianzhong was also captured. All have now been escorted to the capital for interrogation. After questioning, the hostages will be released. The Feng family, who are still at large, are currently being pursued and will be brought to justice once captured.

The widely reported case of Jin Jianxiong and Lu Wanhua, who committed suicide by throwing themselves into the Yangtze River, a case that shocked Yangzhou, has seen the bodies finally surfacing. The man was wearing a Western suit and shirt, while the woman was wearing a short jacket with her hair cut short. Tragic News of a Storm on Honghu Lake 88

On the evening of the twelfth of this month, a sudden storm arose. In Huaiyin,

nineteen out of every ten houses in Yuanji, Zhaoji, Zhuji, and other places in the northern countryside were overturned by the wind. That evening, Honghu Lake in the second district of this county was affected by the storm. The resulting tragedy was even more severe than on land. It is reported that several hundred merchant ships were docked in the harbor of Gaoliangjian. When the wind rose, the masts of the ships snapped, the sails were destroyed, and the ships capsized in the waves, creating an extremely dangerous situation. As a result, twenty-seven ships of various sizes were lost, and many boatmen were drowned. Moreover, nine households near the lake in the water patrol team's quarters were submerged. The most severely affected was the family of Ye Derong, where one woman and three young children died. It was truly a catastrophe.

Local News

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 91

Inquiring About the Norwegian Exclusion of Overseas Chinese 92

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, having heard of Norway’s exclusion of overseas Chinese, yesterday specially cabled the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to inquire about the truth. The text of the cable reads: "To the esteemed Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing: Reports indicate that there are only six overseas Chinese in Norway, half of whom have already been expelled. It is now heard that the remaining three in the country will also continue to be ostracized. Since this news was published, Hansson, the Norwegian Consul General in Shanghai, has issued a denial, published in the local newspapers on August 6th, stating, 'There are only three overseas Chinese in the entire country of Norway, and it is logically impossible for there to be any anti-Chinese actions.' Is it true that there are only six overseas Chinese in Norway? Were the three previously expelled deported on false pretenses, or are there other reasons? The Consul's statement seems to completely dismiss the previous expulsion of the three. Recently, cases such as Mexico’s expulsion of over ten thousand overseas Chinese have occurred, and the Consul of that country in Shanghai has also denied the facts. Such one-sided defenses are inherently untrustworthy. Merely because Mexican business in China lacks deep and reliable foundations, there is no way to deal with it. Norway sells the most paper to our country, which is different from the situation in Mexico. It seems that we cannot listen to their excuses and fabrications. What is the truth? We earnestly request your esteemed Ministry to investigate and inform us. Respectfully, Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

Central News Agency reports: Song Ziwen, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, was ordered on April 18th to travel to the United States to attend President Roosevelt's Economic Talks. He then went to Europe to attend the London World Economic Conference and traveled around Europe to meet with political leaders from various countries. It has been four months and the work has been completed. He departed from Seattle on the President Jefferson on the twelfth of this month and is expected to arrive in Shanghai around the twenty-ninth. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, recognizing Song's contributions to the country, convened representatives from all walks of life at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce at approximately 1:00 p.m. yesterday to discuss ways to prepare for a welcome party. Representatives from over twenty groups attended. The details are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives 95

The representatives who attended included Wang Xiaolai and Zheng Chengqing from the General Chamber of Commerce, Yu Zhongxian and Zhang Yichen from the First Municipal Association of the Shanghai Special District, Hu Fengxiang from the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession, Cheng Zhusun from the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, Jiang Yuan San from the Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff, Xue Guangqian and Liu Xuru from the Joint Association of University Students, Ma Jiazhen and Huang Zaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association, Liu Zirun and Wu Baojin from the Joint Association of Middle School Faculty and Staff, Gao Zongjing and Sun Deming from the Joint Association of Middle School Students, Zhang Kechang and Shui Yunxiang from the Postal Workers Union, Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers Association, Zhu Xuefan and Long Peiyun from the General Labor Union, Huang Gongfu from the National Postal Workers Union, Qian Yuansheng and Yu Zuoting from the Money Trade Association, Yang Youlong from the Shipping Trade Association, Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Fishery Association, Chen Zeqing from the Banking Association, and Chen Peide from the Fifth District Cigarette Industry Association, totaling over thirty people.

Chairman's Report 96

Moreover, Minister Song's efforts in Europe and the Americas have created a new landscape for the country's financial future, on which the nation’s economic interests depend. The citizens of this city, in order to express their gratitude to Minister Song and to gain a true understanding of various issues, must have an extremely enthusiastic and grand welcome party. Therefore, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce has specifically convened all the group representatives here to actively prepare for the welcome, and so on. After the report, Wang left early because he had another meeting, and Zhu Xuefan, the representative from the General Labor Union, took over as chairman.

Matters Discussed 97

(1) Name: How should the name of the association be decided? It was decided to name it "Shanghai All Circles Welcome Minister Song Home Preparatory Committee." (2) Participating groups: In addition to the 21 groups convened by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, should other groups be invited to participate? It was decided that in addition to the 21 groups convened by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the three groups that attended today, the Pacific International Association, the International Problems Research Association, and the National Postal Workers Union, totaling 25 groups, would be the Preparatory Committee. Other groups in the city can freely participate in the welcome party without joining the Preparatory Committee. The resolution was passed. (3) Organization: Regarding the organization of the Preparatory Committee, should the 25 groups in the Preparatory Committee be the standing committee members, or should a few groups be separately selected from the 22 groups to be standing committee members? It was decided to select eleven groups from the twenty-five groups to be committee members. The eleven selected groups are as follows: (1) Municipal Chamber of Commerce, (2) Municipal Farmers Association, (3) Municipal Education Association, (4) Postal Workers Union, (5) Joint Association of University Students, (6) Joint Association of Middle School Faculty and Staff, (7) First Citizen Federation, (8) Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession, (9) Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, (10) Joint Association of Middle School Students, (11) Boy Scouts Council. It was decided that these eleven groups would be the committee members of the Preparatory Committee. (4) Regarding the discussion of the meaning of the welcome, it was decided to divide it into three points: (1) Commending Minister Song's achievements, (2) Inquiring about the actual situation of the various missions undertaken by Minister Song, (3) Expressing the hopes of the citizens for Minister Song. (5) The date and location of the Preparatory Committee were decided. The Preparatory Committee will meet at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce this Sunday (20th) at 2:00 p.m. The meeting adjourned.

(3) Number of representatives to be elected: It was publicly decided to elect 37 people, and immediately elected Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Chen Binghui, Zhu Yangwu, Liu Zhongying, Wang Jingdong, Zhu Baoluo, Qiu Jialiang, Zheng Dongshan, Shen Songtao, Chen Jiujia, Wang Honghui, Wang Hesong, Yu Zhongxian, Liang Nianzhou, Zhang Yumen, Ge Futian, Chen Shuxian, Zhang Zhizeng, Zhang Dufu, Ren Nongxuan, Xing Guxiang, Sun Mingqi, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Zhihao, Lin Kanghou, Kuang Zhongmou, Xu Genghua, Chen Jicheng, Zhu Zhichun, Shen Tianxin, Tao Leqin, Cao Zhigong, Qiu Pingshan, Wang Yansong, Zhang Xianfang, and Wang Hanliang. (4) Number of standing committee members to be elected: It was publicly decided to elect eleven people, and Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Wang Yansong, Wu Zhihao, Kuang Zhongmou, Xu Genghua, Wang Hanliang, Shen Tianxin, and Chen Binghui were immediately mutually elected as standing committee members.

The meeting adjourned around 4:00 p.m.

Anti-War Conference Representatives

Marre et al. Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 99

A Group of Five Resides at the Cathay Hotel

A Final Decision Will Be Made Regarding the Investigation in Northeast China

The five members of the Barbusse Investigation Team attending the World Anti-War Conference arrived in Shanghai at 10:40 a.m. yesterday aboard the French postal ship Andre Lebon. They landed at the China Merchants Bureau Middle Pier and took cars to the Cathay Hotel to rest.

Brief Biographies of the Five Representatives 100

The five representatives who arrived in Shanghai yesterday: (1) The British representative, Lord Marley, Chairman of the Anti-War Association. Lord Marley served as Secretary of State for War during the MacDonald Labour government and also served in the Navy for nineteen years. (2) The British representative, Hamilton, served as the London Times correspondent in Germany. He grew up in Shanghai. He left Shanghai to return to England when he was only three months old and returned to Shanghai again at the age of nineteen. Therefore, he is extremely interested in China. (3) The French representative, Cottrell, is the editor-in-chief of a famous French newspaper. (4) The French representative, Barbusse, is a well-known French writer. (5) The Belgian representative, Matte, once served as the Mayor of Brussels, the capital of Belgium. In addition, Mrs. Cottrell, the wife of the French representative, is visiting China as a tourist and does not have any specific task.

Lord Marley's Speech 101

Lord Marley, Chairman of the Anti-War Conference, told a reporter from this newspaper yesterday on the ship that he plans to visit Japan after the conference. Whether the Barbusse Investigation Team will go to Northeast China for investigation has not been decided yet, but all members of the team are willing to go and observe. The confirmed representatives from various countries attending the conference include those from the UK, USA, France, Belgium, Austria, Canada, and Germany. One representative sent by Germany was arrested, and another is ill. Whether they can attend is still a question. Lord Marley and his party of five are staying at the Cathay Hotel. It is reported that they will stay in Shanghai for three months.

The National Products Factories Association

Submits a Request to the Ministries to Maintain Domestic Steel 103

Implement a Tax on Dumping

The Shanghai National Products Factories Association submitted a joint request to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "We are submitting this request to maintain domestic steel and increase the dumping tax on foreign steel. The association convened a meeting of the Executive Committee on August 15th of this year. Standing Committee Member Zhang Zigeng proposed a motion to maintain domestic steel, stating: 'Our country is rich in mineral resources, especially iron. The earliest and largest-scale iron smelting plant in our country was the Hanyang Iron Works in Hubei. Unfortunately, due to various reasons, it has long been shut down. The only domestic producer left is the reorganized Liuhegou of the Yangtze Plant, with a monthly output of only over 2,800 tons. Now, due to the dumping of foreign steel at prices as low as over fifty taels per ton, it has fallen to twenty-five yuan, which, including other expenses, only amounts to twenty-eight yuan. However, the cost of domestic steel requires sixty-six yuan, a difference of twenty-eight yuan. As a result, the iron ore is in a precarious state and may collapse at any moment. If this continues, it will inevitably close down. The country is based on the people, and the people are based on industry, which in turn is based on iron. The survival of a mine is small, but the interests of the country are greatly affected. If the country has no iron, the foundation of all its industries will be in the hands of others. How can it hope to revitalize itself? Therefore, our colleagues have organized the China Machinery Joint Company and are doing their best to advise the industry to adopt domestic steel. Although the patriotism of various industries may be able to arouse their righteous indignation for a time and encourage them to purchase it enthusiastically, it is not enough to plan for the long term. The only thorough solution is to ask the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance to consider the pain suffered by domestic steel and its impact on the future of industry, and to increase the dumping tax on Japanese iron in accordance with international practice, so as to protect this only remaining domestic steel and benefit the progress of future industries infinitely.' The resolution was passed, transferred, and recorded in the files. It is reasonable to submit this request. We earnestly request your esteemed Ministry to approve our request and consider the pain that foreign steel dumping is obstructing the sales of domestic steel and affecting domestic iron ore, and that it is in danger of being unable to sustain itself. We request that you approve the implementation of a dumping tax in accordance with the Foreign Goods Dumping Tax Law to maintain the sales of domestic iron ore, which would be a public convenience."

Reports on Activities 104

Wu Yicheng, the acting commander-in-chief of the National Salvation Army of China under Wang Delin, sent Wang Haishan as a representative on August 1st, carrying a letter from Wu, secretly entering the Pass to report on military affairs to Commander-in-Chief Wang Delin, and to beg for assistance from all walks of life. Wang Haishan has arrived in Shanghai yesterday and plans to go south to meet Wang Delin. The original letter from Wu Yicheng to Wang Delin is recorded as follows: "Commander-in-Chief, I am sending Wang Haishan to secretly enter the Pass to report on the recent battles and destruction at the front, and to appeal for material assistance in order to resist for a long time. I ordered all brigades on July 1st to launch a general offensive on July 15th, combining all brigades to work together in their respective locations, to do their best to destroy and disrupt. I then assigned the work addresses of each brigade (in secret). After July 20th, I received successive reports from Brigade Commander Qi Shuangsheng, etc. On that day, Brigade Commander Qi destroyed railways and cut down telegraph poles for more than forty li in a certain place, intercepted several trains, killed forty-eight Japanese soldiers, and obtained some supplies and military equipment, achieving considerable victory. On the same day, Li Qingtian reported that on that day, in a certain two places, over 2,000 comrades gathered and burned many houses in both places, causing heavy losses to the Japanese. Koreans rioted in sympathy, but unfortunately, they did not occupy the area. Our army suffered dozens of casualties and then occupied the area. Zhang Yuting reported that after leading a team to destroy the west bridge of a certain six stations, a Japanese military vehicle derailed and fell under the bridge, crushing over a hundred Japanese soldiers.

The Municipal Land Value Tax Is Being Prepared for Collection

The First Half of the Year Saw a Reduction of One-Sixth 105

A Thorough Investigation of Foreign Perpetual Leases Outside the Urban Area 106

The municipal land value tax, although announced by the government, will be collected from August 1st of this year, but due to the cumbersome procedures, it is still difficult to determine when it will begin to be collected. A reporter from the Central News Agency specifically visited the Land Bureau to inquire in detail. The news released by the bureau is as follows:

[

Collection Regulations 107

The Interim Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax in this city have been revised several times and were officially promulgated at the end of July this year. Therefore, although the collection regulations stipulate that the land value tax will be collected twice this year, in July and January, since July has already passed, it has been postponed to be collected from January to August. Therefore, the land value tax to be collected for the first half of this year will be reduced by one-sixth.

Deadline for Filing 108

According to the regulations of the land value tax, the landowners should first report the land value and then submit it to the valuation committee to determine the land value. Currently, the bureau is drawing up forms to distribute to landowners and set a deadline for filing so that the land value can be determined as soon as possible.

Foreign Leased Land 109

Among the urban areas in this city that have been determined to collect land value tax, there is still a part of the land that is perpetually leased by foreigners. According to the collection regulations, the perpetually leased land should pay land value tax in accordance with the regulations. However, since this matter involves Sino-foreign negotiations, the municipal government should notify the consuls of the countries to which the perpetual leaseholders belong and instruct the perpetual leaseholders to report the land value and pay taxes in accordance with the regulations. Therefore, the bureau is currently rushing to investigate the situation of all foreign perpetual leases in the inner city, preparing a list, and submitting it to the municipal government to request each consul to notify the perpetual leaseholders.

No Collection from Farmland 110

As for the part of the farmland in the urban area, it has been decided not to collect land value tax, but to continue to collect land tax. All the farmland tax collection offices originally established in areas such as Hunan District will be closed when the land value tax is collected, and a land value tax collection office will be established separately.

The name and firearms have all been obtained. The telegraph poles and railways at the Seventh and Eighth Stations have all been destroyed. On the same day, Guo, Brigade Commander of a certain area, led a team to destroy many railways and burn bridges. Yao, Brigade Commander and Mrs. Kong, have caused extensive damage to the railways and telegraph poles east of a certain area. The above is a general description of the situation of the various brigades since the battle on the 15th. Details will be reported later. However, our army's ammunition was originally not abundant and lacked a source. Although we obtained a small amount of ammunition from the enemy after this general offensive, it was not enough to replenish half of our needs. Please find a way to provide assistance to resist. Winter clothing should be prepared as early as possible to avoid the suffering of being frozen and hungry for the 100,000 strong. We also ask the Commander-in-Chief to return to defend the country as soon as possible to boost morale, or please ask Deputy Commander Kong to return to defend the country first and lead the effort.

Tomorrow is the anniversary of the martyrdom of revolutionary martyr Liao Zhongkai in Guangdong in the 14th year of the Republic of China. Memorial Methods 112

(1) Convene representatives from all circles in Shanghai to hold the eighth anniversary memorial meeting for martyr Liao Zhongkai. (2) The date is set for August 20th at 9:00 a.m. (3) Location: Third floor of the Municipal Party Department. (4) The chairman of the meeting will be appointed by the Municipal Executive Committee. (5) Starting from August 18th, publish a notice in the newspaper for three days to notify all levels of party departments, as well as all organs, groups, and schools, to send representatives and prepare letters to participate. (6) Order the lower-level party departments to conduct propaganda in accordance with the propaganda points issued by the Central Committee and report the handling situation for verification. We hope that all organs, groups, schools, and all levels of party departments in this city will send two representatives to prepare letters to participate. This notice is hereby issued.

Slogans 114

French Concession

Two Urgent Telegrams from the Chinese Taxpayers' Association 116

Regarding the French Occupation of the Nine Small Islands

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent two telegrams yesterday to the National Government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the French Minister to China, strongly arguing for our country's territorial sovereignty. The two telegrams are transcribed below:

Telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 117

To the esteemed Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in the capital, it is reported that French warships have occupied nine islands belonging to our country's Qiong province, which is a gradual initiation of armed aggression. Public sentiment is extremely indignant. If negotiations are not carried out quickly to recover them, it will inevitably arouse the covetousness of other countries. How can the integrity of our country's territory be guaranteed? If the other party continues to rely on its strength and occupies them for a long time, we should urgently appeal to the League of Nations in order to preserve our territory and maintain sovereignty. We earnestly hope and pray for this. Sincerely, Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association, Xiaoxiao.

Telegram to the French Minister 118

To His Excellency Mr. Wilden, French Minister to China in Beiping, it is reported that warships from your country have occupied nine small islands south of our country's Hainan Island. Our citizens are extremely indignant about this. We sincerely hope that Your Excellency will consider the friendship between China and France, and quickly convey to your government that they respect the integrity of the territories of all member states of the League of Nations, and promptly remove all forms of occupation, in order to maintain the friendship and strengthen the amity. We earnestly hope and pray for this. Sincerely, Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association, Xiaoxiao.

Tang Youren Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 124

Made a Statement

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Central Political Council, returned to Nanjing from Lushan with President Wang (Jingwei). He took the night train to Shanghai the night before last, arriving here at about 8 a.m. yesterday morning. A Central News Agency reporter met with Mr. Tang at his residence in the Yu Garden and made the following remarks:

Luoxun's Mission to Xinjiang According to Tang, Xinjiang is located on the frontier and is very important. Moreover, the region is divided amongst many ethnic groups and religious beliefs, creating an unusually complex situation. The great powers are eyeing the region, engaging in various schemes. By taking advantage of the differences amongst ethnicities and religions, they are attempting to instigate manipulation in order to fulfill their ambitions of aggression. The central government has seen the hidden worries of Xinjiang, compounded by the inconvenience of transportation and the isolation of news. Therefore, Minister Luo (Wen'gan) has been specially dispatched to inspect the situation in the Northwest and prepare for development, and to prevent major problems in the future. During Minister Luo's inspection period, President Wang (Jingwei) will temporarily serve concurrently as Minister of Foreign Affairs. As soon as Minister Luo returns to Nanjing, he will hand over the post. Rumors that Minister Luo will be appointed full-time Minister of Judicial Administration and that President Wang will serve as Foreign Minister for a long time are not true. The rumor that I will be transferred to the post of Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs is also incorrect. As for when Minister Luo will set out, it is difficult to determine at present.

Feng Yuxiang May Enter Nanjing The Xicha Case has now been resolved peacefully, but all the follow-up matters are quite difficult to handle, especially the reorganization and reorganization of the troops. Feng Yuxiang has now arrived in Jinan and may enter Nanjing. As for what title the central government will give Feng, it has not yet been determined, but it is definitely not a military position. The North China war zone has been completely taken over, but there are rampant bandits and administrative difficulties, and the future is not optimistic.

Use of American Cotton and Wheat The use of American cotton and wheat was decided at the Lushan Conference to be entirely for construction expenses. As for the issue of distribution, it will be decided after Minister Song (Ziwen) returns to the country. Rumors that part of the American cotton will be sold to Japanese merchants seem possible from a commercial point of view, but they are definitely not true from a political point of view.

Holding the Fifth National Congress The Fifth National Congress will be held as scheduled. It is heard that the Southwest has telegraphed Nanjing to express its opposition, but I have not seen the telegram myself. As for the rumor that the Southwest will also hold the Fifth National Congress in Guangzhou at the same time, it is definitely not going to happen, because Chen Jitang has strongly opposed it.

Zhang Xueliang Will Not Return for the Time Being Foreign telegrams claim that Zhang Xueliang will return to China before November and that the central government will give him an important position in the Aviation Administration, etc. Tang strongly denied this statement and said that when Wang (Jingwei) and Jiang (Jieshi) met in Lushan, they discussed the matter of Zhang's return to China and both advocated that Zhang should stay abroad for a long time to conduct inspections. The intention was telegraphed to Zhang. As for the rumor that Chen Mingshu will be appointed Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Five Eastern Provinces, I have heard of it before, but I am not very clear about the extent of the current progress.

French Occupation of the Nine Islands Regarding the French occupation of the nine small islands, the central government is still investigating. As for the names and locations of the nine small islands, as far as is known at present, they do not seem to be the small islands in the Xisha Islands. Therefore, a thorough investigation has been initiated. However, this work is very difficult. Once the investigation is clear, if it is indeed our country's territory, we will lodge a serious protest with France. As for the Japanese rumor that the nine small islands are Japanese territory, there is absolutely no basis for it.

Ningo Vice Captain Wang Zhiguang

Transferred to Serve as Inspector of the Pinghai Warship 126

The Total Cost of the Warship is 8 Million Yuan

The Pinghai cruiser, newly built by the Ministry of the Navy, is the largest cruiser in our country's navy, along with the Ningo. Construction began in May of the 20th year of the Republic and has lasted for over a year. In the middle, due to economic reasons, the project was once suspended. Now, under the order of the Ministry, it is being expedited so that it can be launched on time. The Ministry allocates an additional 30,000 yuan per month for construction costs. The required steel plates have already been shipped from England. In order to emphasize the nuclear warship project, the Ministry of the Navy, in addition to the original inspector Zeng Guocheng, has dispatched Wang Zhiguang, Vice Captain of the Ningo warship, as the warship inspector, to assist in the supervision. Wang arrived at his post yesterday after receiving the order. The total cost of the warship is 8 million yuan in national currency.

Ningo Number One Aircraft Flew Yesterday 127

Number Two Aircraft will be Completed Two Months Later

The reconnaissance aircraft on the Ningo cruiser, Ningo Number One, is a surface-type aircraft. The trial flight was held in the sky above Gaochang Temple on the mornings of the day before yesterday and yesterday. Naval Aviation Instructor He Jian and aviator Xu Chengqi took turns piloting, circling several times in the sky above the city and performing various techniques. The aircraft has 150 horsepower, a speed of 80 miles per hour, and an endurance of four hours. In addition, Ningo Number Two is currently being expedited by the Aircraft Manufacturing Plant and is expected to be completed in about two months. Its structure, except for the engine, which is the same as Number One, has been modified in terms of the fuselage to be a foldable type, which can be folded up and stored when not flying, which is very convenient.

North China

Wartime Telegrams Completely Restored 128

However, Qinhuangdao Temporarily Transfers Water and Electricity Fees, and Fees Must be Doubled

A reporter from New Voice News met with the head of Chinese business at the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications yesterday. According to him, after the wartime telegrams in North China were restored by specialists sent by the Ministry, all wartime telegrams in the war zone were completely destroyed by the Japanese army and had to be repaired. Therefore, when the Japanese army withdrew, they immediately sent craftsmen to repair them. Now, the telegrams in Qinhuangdao, Beidaihe, Tangshan, and other places have all been restored. Only Shanhaiguan requires the specialist sent by the Ministry to negotiate with all parties because the Japanese army is stationed there. Although the telegrams in Shanhaiguan are still received and sent as usual, they must be transferred via water lines and the pseudo-Manchukuo, resulting in telegram fees being doubled as usual.

In the shortest possible time, they will also provide services such as handling freight procedures, picking up and sending packages, and handling local specialties.

The Shanghai City General Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the city government yesterday to negotiate the cancellation of telephone charges in the concessions. City General Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram Requesting Explanation

Can Appeals Be Made Against Illegal Penalties for Stamps? 131

The Shanghai City General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Nanjing Judicial Yuan and the Supreme Court yesterday to request an explanation of whether appeals can be made in cases handled by the courts involving stamp taxes. The original text is recorded below: "To the esteemed Judicial Yuan of Nanjing and the Supreme Court, it is noted that the judicial organs, when handling cases of violations of the Stamp Tax Ordinance, do not allow appeals to be filed in accordance with the penalties and implementation rules of the ordinance's Article 4. However, this rule was implemented with the filing of the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Justice in June of the 17th year of the Republic. By the 22nd year of the Republic, the Ministry of Finance approved the adoption of Shandong Province's methods to improve the stamp tax penalty procedures, allowing penalized merchants in each county to state concrete reasons within 15 days and submit them to the provincial bureau for review by the provincial review committee. It is that cases of stamp tax penalties in each county have the right to request a review, while the judicial organs have no way to appeal, which is unreasonable. Or, it is said that the above rules have been implicitly abolished since the Ministry of Finance approved the change, but it is not known whether this view is appropriate. Furthermore, according to the interpretation of the Supreme Court and the instructions of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, if there is a violation of the law in the stamp penalty, the original court can be requested to revoke it. However, it is difficult to guarantee that there will be no preconceived notions when requesting the judge of the original court to revoke it. If the application is still rejected, is it permissible to appeal? It is a matter of great importance. If appeals are not allowed, the higher court cannot question whether the original trial has violated the law in its determination of facts and the application of the law. It is inevitable that there will be no way to correct it, which is not the original intention of the law to allow people to apply for revocation. The above two points concern the interpretation of the law and are of great importance to all the merchants in the city. It is appropriate to request the esteemed court to review and approve it, and give a legal interpretation so that it can be followed, which is for the public convenience. Sincerely, Shanghai City General Chamber of Commerce, Xiaoxiao."

The Mint Can Cast Ingots on Behalf of Factories 134

Sent a Letter to the Silver and Money Industry Association for Notification

The Central Mint sent a letter to the Silver and Money Industry Association and related organizations, stating, "Respectfully, after reviewing the regulations of the Mint Ordinance, this factory is allowed to cast ingots. Therefore, this factory has been conducting a detailed study of the ingot model in recent months, and preparations are now complete. The ingot die has been manufactured and will be sent to the factory for storage within the next week. However, according to the regulations, the fineness of the ingot should be 999/1000. Since this factory refines the gas on its own, we fear that it will be difficult to achieve precision. If the local financial community wants to request this factory to cast ingots, banks should send large ingots with a fineness of 999/1000 to the Central Bank, which will forward them to this factory. We can cast ingots worth 1,000 yuan in national currency on their behalf to meet the needs of the market. This is a special letter for clarification, requesting your review and notification to all Chinese and foreign banks in the association."

Petitioned Yesterday Morning 136

The Industry Union of the Cigarette Industry in the Fifth District, based on a resolution of the Congress of Representatives, petitioned the Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Committee yesterday regarding the unresolved labor-management disputes at the British American Tobacco Factory, requesting arbitration. At 8 a.m. yesterday, they specially sent all members of the Executive Supervisory Committee, Chen Peide, Liu Dehua, Lou Jingguan, Zhang Ziping, Xiang Yangzhou, Hu Xiaomei, Fei Keguang, Xie Peiji, and more than 60 representatives from various departments to petition to the Municipal Government first, and then to the Municipal Party Committee with the same request.

Response from the Municipal Government 137

(2) The case of the three new workers will be handled separately. (3) The unpaid wages for the two days will be submitted to legal arbitration in accordance with the law. (4) The school incident will be discussed again by the Social Bureau. Dai Youheng, a cadre of the People's Training Section of the Municipal Party Committee, met with them. Regarding the workers' requests, he agreed to refer to the Municipal Government's intentions and handle them jointly with the Social Bureau.

The British American Tobacco Company's factory oppresses workers, forcing its way forward step by step, such as refusing to formulate management rules, depriving workers of their interests, refusing to recognize revisions, destroying school contracts, destroying labor education, refusing to mediate, reducing wages for the two days of the strike, refusing to pay, unjustly dismissing three new apprentice workers, refusing to reinstate them. All of the above have been secretly ordered to be mediated, but there has been no result. We request that your government arbitrate. On the 4th of this month, worker No. 46 in the old factory's tobacco leaf department was unjustly dismissed, causing a general strike. All kinds of perverse actions are intentionally provoking the workers. Although the union has repeatedly tried to compromise, it has been unbearable. Now, the union has made a decision at an emergency congress of representatives to submit to the Municipal Government to promptly arbitrate all the unresolved cases mediated by the Social Bureau in accordance with the law, so as to show impartiality. Please record the situation, and hereby submit a report to your government, requesting that the unresolved cases be arbitrated in accordance with the law to avoid the expansion of the disturbances. The Former Anti-Japanese Association Mistakenly Seized National Products

Shanghai Battle Damage Compensation Claim 140

A Letter from the Chinese and Foreign Sundry Goods Industry to the Chamber of Commerce

According to the New Sound Society, the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Sundry Goods Industry Association wrote to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that eleven pairs of Zhong Zhangji's domestically produced "Clear Sky Rainy Day" shoes were mistakenly confiscated by the former Anti-Japanese Association. After investigation, it was confirmed that they were domestic products and the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods issued a notice for their return. However, the goods were stored in the North Warehouse and were destroyed during the January 28th Incident. Therefore, the matter was reported to the Municipal Government and they were no longer to be returned. Furthermore, Wan Xixiang's shoes were confiscated, containing imported English thread, and were ruled as forfeited. The association argued that the goods had been detained for a long time, and the owner had already suffered significant losses. Now, they were not to be returned, which would particularly impact their capital. Therefore, they wrote to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting that the matter be forwarded to the Municipal Government, instructing the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods to provide compensation. The original letter is recorded below:

Respectfully, we received your association's letter No. 3117 Cao, dated July 14th, which stated that on the 14th of this month, we received an order from the Municipal Government, stating that the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods of the former Anti-Japanese Association had submitted a report on the situation of clearing and registering confiscated goods, requesting review. Accordingly, we have checked that this case was previously submitted to the government by the association, and it was forwarded and commented upon. Now, based on the previous situation, in addition to the comment, we are issuing a copy of the submission, ordering the association to be informed, etc. A copy of the submission is attached. We are respectfully sending this letter, hoping that your association will forward it to the relevant parties mentioned therein. We eagerly await your assistance.

In response, we have already notified Zhong Zhangji and Wan Xixiang. Now, Zhong Zhangji has replied, stating that the eleven pairs of "Clear Sky Rainy Day" shoes stored at Ren Dachang had already received Notice No. 166 from the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods of the former Anti-Japanese Association, which stated that it had been resolved that they should be returned. However, due to the goods being stored in the North Warehouse and destroyed, it has been reported to the Municipal Government that they should not be returned, etc. Upon inspection, the identification of the "Clear Sky Rainy Day" shoes was clear, and it was obvious that they were made by Chinese merchants. However, the inspector acted rashly and confiscated the goods. At the time, a statement was made to the Anti-Japanese Association for their return, but the council delayed the matter, and it was not resolved. Later, it was learned that several days before the January 28th Incident, the association had transported the goods from the North Warehouse to a safe place for storage. It is assumed that the "Clear Sky Rainy Day" shoes were also among them. Now, it is known that they have been destroyed and should not be returned. We are deeply dismayed.

If we speak based on the facts, the fault lies with the Anti-Japanese Association, and not with the owner of the goods. This is very clear. Furthermore, merchants operating domestic goods should not suffer losses in vain. The principle of justice is difficult to accept. If we speak based on the law, "Article 767 of the Civil Code states that the owner of property may request the return of property from anyone who illegally possesses or seizes their property, and may request the removal of any obstruction to their property rights." Therefore, the ownership of the goods is granted by law, and cannot be deprived without reason. Now, the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods advocates selling Japanese goods to prepare for repaying the debts owed by the former Anti-Japanese Association, but disregards the non-Japanese goods that were destroyed. This is tantamount to focusing solely on the rights of the association, and not considering its obligations. This is not only unfair, but also fails to fulfill the function of clearing. Appropriate compensation should be given for the non-Japanese goods that were destroyed, so that the owner's capital is secured, and both the law and the facts are taken into consideration, so as not to cause resentment. We sincerely request that this letter be forwarded for implementation.

Furthermore, Wan Xixiang has replied, stating that the confiscated thread is indeed a product of the British Cotton & General Merchants Co. Ltd., which can be proven. To forfeit it suddenly is unfair. Upon investigation, what they stated is indeed insightful. If domestic goods are mistaken for enemy goods, it has already caused the owner to suffer from illiquidity. To not return them and cause them to lose their capital innocently, how can this be explained rationally or emotionally? If compensation can be given, it would be appropriate. Otherwise, it will cause endless complaints, which is contrary to the original intention of resisting Japan.

Based on the aforementioned circumstances, we have prepared this letter and respectfully submit it. We hope that your association will quickly forward it to the Municipal Government for approval and to the Committee for Clearing Confiscated Goods to handle the matter as requested. We greatly value our public duty.

Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Water Recedes Slightly in Central Henan

Passenger Trains on the Pinghan Railway Have Resumed 142

Due to the rising waters of the Yellow River in recent days, several spans of the Yellow River Railway Bridge on the Pinghan Railway were submerged, preventing train traffic. Yesterday, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration received a telegram from the Pinghan Railway Management Committee stating that the floodwaters of the Yellow River in central Henan had receded slightly and that passenger trains on the Pinghan Railway had resumed operations on the 16th. However, the Yellow River Railway Bridge is leaning and has not yet been repaired, so freight trains are still not running.

Silk Factories Still Face Difficulties in Returning to Normal 143

After the new silkworm cocoons came onto the market, the silk industry in this city saw silk prices soar due to brisk sales to Europe and America, and the number of factories that resumed operations temporarily accounted for 40-50% of the total. Subsequently, sales to Europe declined again, and prices also fell. In addition, labor strikes broke out in silk factories in the Pudong and Zhabei districts, and factories successively suspended operations. By the time the wage issue was resolved, a total of only 43 silk factories citywide were operating. However, overseas silk sales remained sluggish, and the amount of silk stored in various factories increased daily. They all took advantage of the summer vacation to reduce working hours, only working half days in the morning. Now that autumn has arrived and the weather is cool, silk factories should normally resume full-day operations. However, European and American silk sales have suffered a setback, and telegrams report that silk prices are more than 200 yuan lower than the highest price in summer. Furthermore, there are no large-scale transactions, and the silk stored in various factories cannot be sold. Therefore, it is difficult for factories to return to normal operations in the short term.
