Ministry Order to Calibrate Weighing Scales 146

150 Sets to be Made

Issued for Use on Various Railways

The Joint Transportation Department of the Ministry of Railways stipulates in the Joint Transportation Regulations and the General Rules for Freight Car Transportation that excess weight of luggage and parcels within 5% and excess weight of goods within 2% are exempt from additional freight charges. However, in reality, due to the inaccuracy of the weighing scales and the cleverness of the consignors, the recorded weight of ordinary goods and freight tickets often exceeds 5%, and the excess weight of joint transportation luggage and parcels often exceeds 10%. Based on this statistic, the amount of freight losses nationwide must be alarming. Even if we take the national freight revenue and joint transportation luggage and parcel revenue for the year 20 as the standard, the annual losses due to excess weight are estimated to be over 3 million yuan. Even if we estimate it at one-third, the amount is still over one million yuan.

However, the reasons for the inaccuracy of the weighing scales on various railways are nothing more than the following:

Zhao Youming's Private Morphine Manufacturing Case

Appeal to the Supreme Court Rejected 147

The Third Trial Concludes, Upholding the Original Verdict 148

Sentenced to Three Years Imprisonment and a Fine of 5,000 Yuan

Zhao Youming (also known as Zhao Yumin and Zhao Picheng), the former Yunnan negotiator, resided in Shanghai after leaving office and worked as an agent in the political department of a certain organization. He privately set up a morphine manufacturing facility on the third floor of a foreign house at No. 121 Yao Zhu Jiao Road in the French Concession. On June 11th of last year, the Chinese and foreign detectives of the French Concession police raided the facility and arrested the accomplices Hou Yunshan, Liu Mingzhang, Hou Lihe, Gan Hongfa, Jin Yushan, etc., who were taken to the police station for detention. The next day, Zhao surrendered himself to the police station, intending to plead for leniency, but he was detained and charged with initiating the Second Special District Court. After interrogation, Zhao was sentenced to three years imprisonment and a fine of 5,000 yuan. The others were sentenced to imprisonment and fines. Zhao and others disagreed and appealed to the Higher Third Branch Court, but the appeal was rejected. Zhao and others then appealed to the Supreme Court, which also rejected the appeal and upheld the original verdict. This was reported in previous newspapers.

It is now learned that this case has concluded after three trials and the verdict has been finalized. In the morning of the previous day, Judge Guo Dezhang of the Higher Third Branch Court opened an execution court and brought Zhao and the others to the court. After a brief interrogation, he instructed that the number of days of detention before the discount was decided and ordered them to be sent to prison for execution and to pay the fines within a limited time. After the instructions, the bailiffs escorted Zhao and the others to the Second Special District Prison on Masnan Road to carry out the following two points.

Different Types and Used for Too Long 149

1. The scales are of different types, and the employees may not be familiar with the methods of use and protection. (2) They have been used for too long and have lost their flexibility.

In order to remedy the above defects, the Joint Transportation Department sent technician Li Yue to investigate the Bureau of Weights and Measures of the Ministry of Industry. From the certified weighing scales and weights manufactured by the bureau, 18 items were selected. After verification, 150 sets were ordered for use at major stations. At the same time, referring to the Implementation Regulations for Weights and Measures of the Ministry of Industry and the Method for Checking Weights and Measures Instruments for Public Use, nine articles on unified railway weighing scale calibration methods were drafted and submitted to the Minister for approval. The Ministry then issued Instruction No. 6164 of the Joint Transport Department, ordering all railways to comply. The Two Railway Administrations will dispatch 20 sets of the said weights. After they are received, they will be distributed to major stations for trial use.

Unified Standard Weighing Scale Method

1. In order to unify the kilogram weighing scales at all railway stations, the Ministry of Railways has ordered the Joint Transportation Department to formulate standard weights for use at all stations. (2) Each set of standard weights consists of 18 pieces, weighing two pieces of one gram, one piece of two grams, one piece of five grams, ten pieces of one kilogram, and four pieces of ten kilograms, totaling 50 kilograms and 9 grams. In order to facilitate storage, three wooden boxes are specially made to store them separately. (3) The employees responsible for the safekeeping of the weighing scales at each station shall carefully preserve these weights and not allow them to rust, which would cause changes in weight. (4) The weighing scales shall be calibrated in accordance with the procedures for the inspection of platform scales in Article 25 of the Method for Checking Weights and Measures Instruments for Public Use of the Ministry of Industry. (5) When calibrating the weighing scales, in addition to the provisions previously stipulated, the weighing scales shall first be cleaned and checked to see if they are placed level and whether the four wheels are in contact with the ground. Then, place one one-kilogram weight on the weighing pan to check the accuracy. Then, gradually add one kilogram weights and check each kilogram. When there is a difference, it should be registered immediately. Record how many grams the weight is more or less at a certain number of kilograms. When adding up to ten kilograms, remove all the one-kilogram weights and replace them with a ten-kilogram weight. Then, use one-kilogram weights to gradually increase them one by one and check them successively. When adding up to 50 kilograms, remove all the weights and replace them with a bucket of water of the same weight or other items. Then add the weights one kilogram at a time, and so on, and the weight can be increased to any weight.

The Weighing Scale Used Must be Flexible

1. The stationmasters and weighing scale personnel at each station should study and understand the function of each part of the weighing scale, and lubricate and oil them at any time to make them flexible. If placed outdoors, they should be covered with oilcloth after use to protect them. (7) Each railway should have at least one-tenth of the reserve weighing scales stored in the repair shop for the use of each station's request for repair and replacement. When each station requests repairs, the spare weighing scale should be sent first. Once the weighing scale to be repaired is sent, it must be repaired quickly for replacement by other stations. For roads with longer routes, spare weighing scales can be stored in several places. (8) If these weights are damaged and cannot be used, each station should state the reasons and submit them to the road in charge for verification and transfer to the Joint Transportation Department for replacement. (9) If there are any matters not covered in these measures, they may be submitted to the Ministry for revision at any time.

Fire Conditions in this City

Zhabei District is More Advanced than Before the War

Preliminary Plan Formulated for the City Center

The construction of fire prevention facilities in this city has always been emphasized. Although the fire brigades in Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and other districts suffered great losses after the January 28th Incident, they have recently been restored to their original state. A reporter from the Central News Agency went to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to inquire about the current situation of fire prevention in this city. According to Dong Zhihe, director of the Fire Department of the bureau, the details are as follows:

Zhabei Restored to Original State

Originally, Zhabei District had the most successful fire prevention work in this city. Although it suffered a major blow after the Shanghai War, it has now been restored to its original state and is even more advanced than before. Zhabei District is divided into four sections, and the fire brigades in three of these sections have sophisticated equipment and skilled techniques, making them second to none in Shanghai. The fire brigade in that section originally had five pumper fire trucks, and recently ordered a new British-style pumper truck worth about 50,000 yuan. The truck is equipped with a 60-foot-high ladder, so even if the tallest buildings are on fire, the fire brigade in that section can still go to the rescue. In addition, the Zhabei Fire Brigade Association has recently purchased an ambulance, which is also very well equipped and is specially prepared for the rescue of victims in the event of a fire. Since it was put into trial use, the results have been excellent.

Gradual Expansion in Various Districts

As for the Hubei South District, it remains in its normal state. The Gaoqiao and Yangjing districts still use old-fashioned fire-fighting equipment due to various reasons. However, the bureau is actively trying to expand and reform them. The Lan Ni Du area of ​​Pudong has a dense population and frequent fires. Although the fire-fighting equipment used is more complete than the two districts mentioned above, it cannot achieve great results due to the inconvenience of water supply. The original fire-fighting equipment in Wusong District was almost completely destroyed in the January 28th Incident, but a new-style pumper fire truck and more than 1,000 feet of leather hose have now been purchased. It will be gradually expanded in the future. Fire prevention in the city center is also being planned, but due to the shortage of municipal funds, the preliminary plan can only be simplified. Fire hydrants will first be installed in places where there are water pipes on various roads, and then a fire brigade will be organized in the area. In the future, it is also planned to transfer some fire-fighting equipment and firefighters from Zhabei District to serve in the area. In addition, the municipal government will allocate several thousand yuan to purchase other essential equipment.

Cracking Down on Incendiary Residents

Because Chinese and foreigners live together in this city and people's hearts are not united, there are often cases of deliberate arson in order to seek illicit wealth. Therefore, the bureau has now drafted registration rules for fire insurance customers to strictly prevent this kind of malpractice. If such incidents occur, they will be severely punished. The rules have now been submitted to the municipal government for review.

In addition, there are so-called "public assessment firms" in this city, which are entrusted by insurance companies. Whenever insured customers encounter fire insurance, they are led by Westerners and several workers to go to the fire site to steal and move items from the households. However, this often leads to the mistaken removal of items from non-insured households, and even hinders fire-fighting work. Therefore, the bureau has recently formulated rules for the collection of public assessment firms at fire sites to restrict them. Once approved and announced by the municipal government, they will be implemented immediately.

Chinese Woman from Kobe Smuggles Gold Bars

Embezzled by Handlers 150

Gold Bars Worth 16,000 Yuan

Sold for Only 7,400 Yuan for Distribution

｜All Persons Involved Arrested One After Another｜

A woman named Huang Jiang opened a restaurant in Kobe, Japan, and accumulated wealth. Recently, because Japan banned the export of gold, the price of gold was lower than elsewhere. The woman secretly sold gold bars to seek huge profits. On June 29th of this year, the American Da Lai Foreign Firm's world liner "Hayes" set sail from Kobe and sailed to Shanghai. Huang Jiang entrusted seven gold bars worth 16,000 yuan to Zhao Chunbao, a typist on the ship, to take to Shanghai and instructed him to give them to Zhu A Cai for receipt. On July 3rd, the Hayes arrived in port. Unexpectedly, Zhao became greedy and embezzled the gold goods with Feng and Ji Li, an old woman in her sixties who lived at No. 343 Xin Tang Jia Lane. The woman's husband, Ji Chunyuan, secretly sold them, obtaining 7,400 yuan for distribution.

Recently, Huang Jiang learned of this and entrusted Heng Rongbao, who worked with Zhao Chunbao, to investigate. Heng learned that Zhao was hiding in the local government district. On the previous day, he reported it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which dispatched detective leader Gu Liancheng and detectives Hu Kuisheng and Gong Fujin to rush to the scene and arrest Zhao. According to his confession, Feng was also living in the same house as Ji Li. Detective Gu and others contacted the Concession Police and dispatched patrolman Ji Xiucai to go to the address to arrest him. However, Feng had heard the news and escaped, and only Ji Li was arrested. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Liu Yugui interrogated them. Detective Gu brought the suspect Zhao to the court and requested permission to bring Ji Li back to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. However, the police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, requested that the woman be temporarily detained, saying that the content of this case was extremely complex, not only involving gold bars, but also possibly involving the abduction and sale of people. Therefore, the police station needs to conduct a detailed investigation. Moreover, the Public Security Bureau's request for transfer has not yet been formally received by the court, and the procedures are still lacking. He requested that Ji Li be sent to prison for investigation. Judge Liu then approved the detention and postponed the hearing for seven days, pending further review after the Public Security Bureau's written request.

Pudong

Continued Report on Relief Efforts for the Lao Bai Du Fire Disaster 151

The China Jisheng Association, Xinwei Relief Association, and China Morality Society jointly organized urgent relief efforts for the Lao Bai Du fire disaster in Pudong. The Xinwei Relief Association donated 1,000 yuan and 6,000 pieces of single clothing. The Morality Society donated 500 yuan, and the Jisheng Association was responsible for the rest. The Jisheng Association sent personnel Li Yunmen and others to investigate. The situation was extremely tragic. On the 17th of this month, relief items were distributed at the Yu Family Temple in Pudong. The Xinwei Relief Association sent personnel to distribute them together, and the Public Security Bureau of the district sent police to maintain order. On that day, relief funds were distributed in three grades: A, B, and C. Grade A was given to 39 households at 6 yuan per household, totaling 234 yuan. Grade B was given to 234 households at 5 yuan per household, totaling 1,170 yuan. Grade C was given to 349 households at 4 yuan per household, totaling 1,396 yuan. There was also a special grade given to one household for 10 yuan. In total, 623 households received a total of 2,810 yuan. In addition, 6,000 pieces of single clothing, 800 bottles of Jisheng Dan, 500 bottles of Jisheng Water, 100 bottles of Baoan Dan, and 100 bottles of Dianyan Shasha San were distributed. These disaster victims were able to temporarily maintain their current situation through this relief.

Municipal Public Works Bureau

Renewed Street Light Contract with Yappuer 152

The Public Works Bureau has always used foreign goods for street lights in the city. In 19, the former director Huang Boqiao found that the domestic Yappuer light bulbs were of very good quality and could match foreign goods. Therefore, the street lights were changed to use Yappuer bulbs. It has been several years and they have been quite satisfied. Special Tobacco Tax Facilitates Merchants

Susong Tobacco Industry Requests Exceptional Supplement

Rejected by the Consolidated Tax Office Yesterday

The Ministry of Finance's Consolidated Tax Office changed the tobacco leaf tax to a special tax and the liquor tax to a fixed amount tax, which has been implemented since July 1st. Although the merchants once expressed dissent, there was no problem. The Susong Tobacco Industry Association and others requested that the newly ordered special tax rate for domestic tobacco leaves be exceptionally supplemented, which was also rejected by the office yesterday and was widely informed to all places. The order is as follows:

In order to implement the order, we have now received a joint telegram from the Susong Tobacco Industry Association and others, requesting that the newly ordered special tax rate for domestic tobacco leaves be supplemented exceptionally to alleviate the merchants' difficulties, etc. The abolition of public sales fees and taxes and the implementation of special taxes for domestic tobacco leaves in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian were originally intended to simplify the process and facilitate merchants. The special tax rate set at 4 yuan and 1 jiao and 5 fen per 100 catties of national currency is nothing more than a merger of the previous collection of public sales fees and taxes, unified collection, and sales anywhere in the special tax area after one collection is sufficient, without repeated collection. The customs transit tax is also allowed to be waived.

The Provisional Regulations for the Collection of Special Tax on Domestic Tobacco Leaves have been promulgated by the Ministry and distributed to the competent bureaus and offices of each province, and shall be followed uniformly from July 1st of this year. Compared with the previous public sales fee and tax, which was based on the province as a unit, if the tobacco leaves were transported to other provinces for sale after the public sales fee and tax had been collected at the production and sales location, the fee and tax still had to be paid in the sales province. It is very clear that it benefits tobacco merchants. How can the merchants misunderstand and want to change the tax system based on the special situation of tobacco leaf production and sales in a corner of the country?

In response to the telegram, we are copying the original telegram and ordering you to inform and notify it immediately. This order.

Bali Bridge Road

Rent Reduction for Houses Along the Road 153

Tongren Fuyuan Hall Sympathizes with Tenants

The houses along Bali Bridge Road and Ningbo Road in the French Concession are owned by Tongren Fuyuan Hall. After the houses were rebuilt last year, most of the houses along Ningbo Road were established as hospitals, while those along Bali Bridge Road were mostly small inns and shops selling groceries, tobacco, paper, and food. Since then, due to the sluggish market in recent years, it has been difficult for the tenants to maintain their current situation by paying such high rents. They have repeatedly convened all the tenants to discuss and request the landlord to reduce the rent burden. After months of negotiations, the landlord has now found that the market is indeed sluggish and has agreed to accept the rent reduction terms.

It is reported that as a result of the negotiations, the original rent of each house along Bali Bridge Road was 80 yuan, but it has now been reduced by 20 yuan to 60 yuan per house. The rents set for the houses along Ningbo Road were not uniform at the time because the houses were of different sizes. It is now agreed to reduce them by 20 percent. The original rent was 100 yuan (proportional), but now 80 yuan will be charged. Yesterday afternoon, the tenants convened a final meeting and were all satisfied, believing that their request for rent reduction had been victorious.

Passenger Dies on Shanghai-Hangzhou Train 154

Cheng Yunhuan, a 40-year-old man from Anhui Province who resided at No. 354 Zhao Jia Road, worked as a waiter at the Zui Hong Lou restaurant in the Yimiao area of Fangbang Road. He usually left home early and returned late, which was his habit. However, because Cheng Yunhuan had been doing business in Shanghai for many years and had not yet returned to his hometown, he missed his hometown very much. Therefore, he and his wife, Cheng Zhang (34 years old), took a rickshaw to the South Railway Station at 7:00 a.m. yesterday, carrying luggage and bought two third-class train tickets to Hangzhou at 7:50 a.m. to return to their hometown. Unexpectedly, Cheng had just boarded the train and sat down when his face suddenly turned pale, he muttered to himself, became unconscious, and barely breathed. Suddenly, his mouth became fixed and his eyes were blank, and he died on the train.

When the railway police saw this, they carried the body down, and the train started to move. They immediately notified the Gaochangmiao Branch of the Second District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and reported to the court to inspect the body. They also forwarded the previous situation to the district chief Jin Tian and submitted it to the General Bureau for record.

Shao Deliang, from Ningbo, was 32 years old and lived at No. 104 Taoyuan Lane, Pei'er Road. He used to run a restaurant in Japan. Sentenced for Assault and Battery After Failed Loan Attempt

Chen Yunti, from Changzhou, used to work at the Da Lun Silk Factory at No. 36 Hongqing Lane, Baoding Road. Recently, he was dismissed from his job due to excessive gambling and prostitution and became unemployed. Due to financial difficulties, at around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, he went to the Da Lun Silk Factory to borrow 3,000 yuan from his former teacher, Lu Weixia from Danyang, claiming that he wanted to open a silk factory. When the loan was denied, he became angry and slapped Lu in the face and tried to punch him. Lu was old and could not defend himself, so he went upstairs to avoid him. Polish National

Drug Trafficking Appeal Pending Judgment 158

Two Polish nationals, Vinski (transliteration) and Xibonski (transliteration), previously asked translator Ding Shouxiang to find customers to sell the drug heroin, hoping to defraud money. Wang Zhihao, Chinese detective No. 85 of the French Concession Police, learned of this and pretended to be a buyer. The two Polish nationals indeed arrived with Ding in a car, bringing seven jars of genuine goods and a wooden box containing 585 pounds of mackerel (falsely represented as heroin). They urgently demanded payment, and were all arrested and taken to the police station and sent to the Second Special District Court, accused of drug trafficking and fraud. They were sentenced to three months in prison and fined 400 yuan each for jointly selling opium substitutes. Ding Shouxiang was sentenced to two months in prison and fined 30 yuan for assisting in the sale. The rest of the charges were acquitted. These details have been previously reported. Now, it is known that Vinski and Xibonski have appealed the original judgment and hired Russian lawyer Wei Wei to file an appeal with the Third Branch of the High Court. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Zhou, along with Judges Guo and Chu, Prosecutor Zhang, held a joint hearing. After mutual arguments between the police lawyer and the appellant's lawyer, the court declared the debate closed and scheduled a date for sentencing.

Tragic Drowning While Swimming at the Beach

Liu Huayue, an 18-year-old student from Suzhou Provincial High School, came to Shanghai during the summer vacation. Police Arrest Gamblers

Verdict in the Case of Drowning Villager 161

In the case of the drowning of villager Zhu Quanlin, which occurred on the afternoon of June 23rd this year in Huijiao, a place in the western township of this county, when the police arrested gamblers, Zhang Rong, the director of the Maqiao Township Public Security Bureau, patrol leader Xie Fengshan, and police officers Jiang Shouen, Xu Enpei, Hua Ke Gong, and Wang Lizhang, were all investigated by the District Court Prosecutor's Office and prosecuted for murder. The debate has ended and the verdict is awaited. It is now known that Judge Yang Qianchang specially opened the Third Court yesterday to announce the verdict. After taking his seat at 10:00 AM, he ordered the detention of Zhang Rong, Xie Fengshan, Jiang Shouen, and Xu Enpei, as well as Hua Ke Gong and Wang Lizhang, who were out on bail, to be brought to the case. After a brief interrogation, he announced the verdict in court. Xie Fengshan and Jiang Shouen were each sentenced to one year of imprisonment for joint negligence causing death. Zhang Rong, as a bureau member, had the responsibility of command and supervision and could not escape blame. He and Hua Ke Gong were each fined 200 yuan. Xu Enpei and Wang Lizhang were both acquitted. As for the private prosecution, a judgment of 1,000 yuan was awarded, to be borne jointly by Xie Fengshan, Jiang Shouen, Zhang Rong, and Hua Ke Gong, each responsible for 250 yuan. The judge said, "The deceased, Zhu Quanlin, had an 83-year-old mother above him and a wife and three daughters below him, a family of five who depended on the deceased for their livelihood. For the sake of prudence, this court repeatedly conducted on-site investigations to clarify the facts. The bereaved family requested 2,120 yuan in compensation, which was not too much. Now, this court has decided to award 1,000 yuan. If anyone is dissatisfied with the judgment, they may appeal." He then ordered Xie Fengshan, Zhang Rong, and Jiang Shouen to be taken back into custody. Xu Enpei was sent to the Prosecutor's Office for temporary detention. Hua Ke Gong and Wang Lizhang were returned to their original guarantors.

Sandboat Encounters Wind and Robbery 162

Cargo Looted

One Crew Member Killed

The Beiyang class "Gong Shun Li" sandboat of Jiangyin Peng Yue Ji Sandboat Company recently loaded northern goods such as salted fish from Shanghai Yi Tai Xiang Ji and other companies in Andong Dalian and set sail for Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 11th of this month, when sailing to the Qingkou Shidao Mountain sea area, a hurricane struck, and the waves crashed against the boat. Two crew members working on the bow were swept away by the waves. The boat owner, Yang Bao, saw this and immediately instructed the helmsman to sail towards the coast. The boat was already close to the coast, when a Qingji steamship also sailed towards the coast, coming head-on. Seeing this, the steamship quickly turned the rudder to avoid it, but the Qingji steamship was traveling fast and collided with the left side of the bow of the "Gong Shun Li." Boat owner Yang Bao inspected the boat and saw that the bow was slightly damaged, but not severely, so he sailed to the coast to anchor. After the wind and waves calmed down, he set sail again. However, after sailing past Shidao Mountain, the bow of the boat was shaken by the waves, and the place where the bow had been hit gradually flooded. When they realized it, the bow cabin was already flooded to a height of five or six feet. The crew was extremely frightened. Boat owner Yang immediately ordered the sails to be lowered and anchored there to observe. There were several cracks in the collision site. He instructed the crew members to use leather belts to pump the water out of the cabin in order to repair the cracks and stop the water. After two days, the repairs were not yet complete. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 13th, near dark, two large three-masted pirate ships suddenly arrived. There were fifty or sixty pirates on board, who swarmed onto the boat, carrying guns and crowding into boat owner Yang's room, demanding that he hand over the silver dollars. Seeing the large number of pirates, Yang had no choice but to hand over more than six hundred silver dollars. The pirates then searched the crew members one by one, taking all the silver dollars. Still not satisfied, they opened the cargo hold and forced the crew members to load the cargo onto the two pirate ships. One crew member was unable to carry cargo due to illness and was shot to death by the pirates. The cargo was looted and loaded onto the two pirate ships. The pirates all jumped onto the pirate ships and sailed away. Boat owner Yang arrived in Shanghai yesterday by steamer and reported to Yi Tai and other companies that the cargo had been looted, worth more than 40,000 yuan. Yi Tai and other companies have now telegraphed the relevant naval and land authorities to arrest and investigate the matter.

He had two sons, the eldest named Pin Cai, 30 years old, who made a living pulling a rickshaw, and the younger named Pin Fu, 19 years old, who worked as a tough laborer carrying cowhide. Woman Suspects Husband of Having an Affair

Suicide by Poison After an Argument 163

Chen Miao, a 39-year-old woman from Yangzhou, committed suicide by poison after an argument with her husband. Her husband, Chen Dechun, worked as a servant for a foreigner at No. 71 Hongye Garden on Yuyuan Road. As a result, the couple resided there. Recently, Mrs. Chen suspected her husband of having an affair with a maid named Wang Ji. On the morning of the previous day at around 9:00 AM, the two had a major argument. Famous Indian Fish Circus Arrives in Shanghai

In recent years, the entertainment industry has seen increasing innovation. We have become accustomed to circuses, dog shows, flea circuses, and animal shows and no longer find them surprising. Now, a so-called "fish circus" has arrived from India, making its debut in China. Commanded by a British man named Aralamania (transliteration), it features several exotic fish. These fish are very different from those commonly seen in our country and are highly combative. Upon contact, they are relentless and fight fiercely, displaying a wide range of fighting techniques, including earth-shattering and mountain-overturning maneuvers. These fighting styles are rare and remarkable even to modern zoologists. It is said that they gave an informal performance at the Royal Theatre in England a few years ago. The audience, consisting of British nobles, paid exorbitant prices to request a performance by the fish circus. All were astounded, speechless, and filled with endless wonder. The troupe passed through Hong Kong and has now arrived in Shanghai, staying temporarily at the Cangzhou Hotel. They plan to perform at a major theater in Shanghai in the near future. It is expected that the price will be high, but the people of Shanghai, driven by curiosity, will empty the streets to compete for a viewing.

Bond sales have exceeded 1,000. Fearing that latecomers will miss out, the office has telegraphed France to purchase more. It is reported that a new batch will arrive in the coming days.

▲ Omega Watch's Honor The squadron led by Italian Air Minister Balbo, which set a round-trip flight record between Rome and Chicago, had carefully planned in advance. In terms of timing, accuracy and reliability were also crucial. Therefore, they purchased various timing devices and split-second timers from Omega, installing them in the 24 aircraft participating in the flight. Omega watches were also purchased for the pilots to wear. The Ministry of Aviation specially appointed Omega as its exclusive watch manufacturer. Omega was designated as the standard timer for the Olympic Games in Los Angeles last year. In the Geneva Observatory chronometer competition, Omega set three world records and won 20 medals. It is reported that the manager for China and Hong Kong is Baoxin Foreign Firm, located at No. 320 Jiangxi Road in this city.

▲ Shanghai Art Supplies Company Recent News The Shanghai Art Supplies Company, located at No. 440 Caishi Road in the French Concession of this city, has been established for over 20 years. It specializes in selling art supplies from various countries and has long been praised by the art community. Since Mr. Liu Hairuo took over as manager, he has worked diligently to expand the business, giving it a new look. Recently, a large shipment of new-style art supplies has arrived from famous European and American factories. They are being sold at discounted prices to suit the economic situation of our country. As the autumn school season is approaching, schools and art groups from this city and other places are flocking to purchase supplies. They are overwhelmed with customers.

▲ Shanghai National Products Company Establishes Discount Market The Shanghai National Products Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, has been implementing its expansion plan since the 1st of this month, managed by the Business Development Committee. The renovation and installation of equipment in various departments of the store is being carried out separately. The committee, in order to attract attention from all sectors of society, has established a discount market on the ground floor as part of the expansion work. Daily national products are displayed in bundles, with prices fixed at two, four, six, eight cents, and one dollar and five types. All are extremely cheap and practical.

▲ New Plan of Zhendan Silk Weaving Company Zhendan Silk Weaving Company in Daomaoxiang, Qingchun Road, Hangzhou, recognizes that ever since frequent ocean voyages have brought European and American silk fabrics that are praised for their novelty, Chinese people eager for modern styles have been purchasing them, leading to a decline in the sales of domestically produced silk. The company, with the aim of improving domestic silk fabrics and reversing this trend, is rapidly catching up. Despite many hardships, they have never slackened their efforts. Over the past ten years, they have expanded extensively, producing hundreds of varieties that are popular with Chinese people and compatriots abroad. Recently, in order to make further improvements, they have advertised in various Shanghai newspapers, soliciting designs for the autumn and winter seasons, hoping to gather the crystallizations of many artists and promote national products. It is reported that since the advertisement was published, there has been an enthusiastic response. After the closure of several large factories in Hangzhou, such as Diwei Cheng, the company has become the largest and most well-organized silk factory. The manager is Mr. Shi Chunshan.

▲ Calligrapher Xu Tiefeng Arrives in Shanghai Mr. Xu Tiefeng followed General Wu Peifu for many years, selling his calligraphy in Tianjin and Beijing, where he gained a high reputation. He has great talent and works diligently, excelling in seal script, official script, regular script, running script, and cursive script. Medical Circle

▲ Sanitation Measures for Flood-Affected Areas Seeing the recent floods in various places, the Wuzhou Pharmacy is concerned that after the floodwaters recede, the accumulation of filth will breed diseases. In order to raise awareness of hygiene in the disaster areas and prevent the spread of disease, they offer the following suggestions: (1) Quickly rinse all parts of the house with clean water and then sprinkle with "Yalin Stink Water" for sterilization and disinfection. (2) Inject "Feiersheng" indoors. If there are mosquitoes and flies, light "Earth Brand Mosquito Repellent Incense" to prevent poisonous insects from biting and spreading germs. (3) If you suffer from dizziness, vomiting, or nausea, take "Liangdan" or inhale "Wen Sha Yao." If you have a fever or chills, take Earth Brand Quinine. Taking these precautions can prevent danger.

Whether it is redness, swelling, granular conjunctivitis, red eyes, or pterygium, all are immediately cured after treatment. Important News 164

Jiangsu Sends Students Abroad 165

Exam Questions Entirely in Chinese

▲ Physical Examinations on the 21st

Jiangsu Province is selecting government-funded students to study in Europe and America. The examinations are being held in Shanghai, as previously reported. Director Zhou of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education convened the first meeting of the examination committee yesterday at the Juelin Villa on Xiafei Road in Shanghai, specifically because the examination period was near. Many important matters were resolved. The following is a summary: 1. Physical examinations will be held at the National Shanghai Medical College on Haige Road from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM on the 21st. 2. Due to the time constraints of the examination, the number of questions may be determined at the discretion of the examination committee. 3. The exam questions will be entirely in Chinese. Specialized terms will be annotated with English. 4. Answers will be mainly in Chinese. 5. The exam questions for each subject will be sealed and submitted to the committee office two days before the examination. The office will send personnel to collect them. 6. The committee members will arrive on time to supervise the examination for the main subjects. 7. Candidates are allowed to bring pens, ink, drawing instruments, and slide rules into the examination hall. 8. Candidates are not allowed to ask questions in the examination hall. 9. The location for grading the papers is at Jiaotong University. Grading will be done as the exams are taken. 10. Scores for each subject will be calculated as a percentage. 11. A second meeting will be held at Juelin Villa at 11:00 AM on the 31st of this month. 12. Mr. Chen Shujuan was additionally elected as a standing committee member.

Cuiying Middle School outside Changmen has been operating for nearly 40 years and is one of the earliest schools in Suzhou. Yesterday was the final day of the literacy campaign launched by the Municipal Citizen Education Center. Municipal Supplementary Schools to Open on Schedule

▲ Scheduled for the 23rd of This Month

The Municipal Supplementary Schools have been operating for six sessions since 1927. This session will be expanded, with a total of 19 schools. The original First Central Supplementary School has been reorganized into the First Vocational Supplementary School, which is exclusively for boys and focuses on commercial subjects. A Second Vocational Supplementary School has been added, which is exclusively for girls and focuses on domestic arts and crafts. This session adds three ordinary supplementary schools, for a total of seventeen. The curriculum includes civics, Chinese, arithmetic, bookkeeping, and natural sciences. They are exclusively for young men and women with some literacy skills (those who are illiterate can attend the Municipal People's School). Tuition is free, and books and supplies are provided. Classes are held from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM. The Municipal Supplementary Schools will open on August 23rd (the opening of the Second Vocational Supplementary School has been postponed due to preparations). Those who wish to supplement their education may enroll at the nearest school. The addresses of the schools are listed below: First Vocational Supplementary School: Located inside the Nongtan Elementary School, Hugunying. Second Vocational Supplementary School: Located on Yisu Street, in the city. First Supplementary School: Located inside the Dongming Elementary School, Fuyou Road. Jiangnan College Seeks Expansion

▲ Remarks by Dean Lin Zhongke

Jiangnan College in this city, since Chen Lifu, Wu Xingya, and others joined as directors, has been striving to expand its content and development. Recently, enrollment has been very enthusiastic. According to Dean Lin Zhongke, the various specialized departments offered by the college this term, such as rural economics and reclamation, are not available at any other universities in Shanghai, and they are urgently needed at present. China's rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. We believe that to save China, we must first save the countryside. To save the countryside, talent is the first priority. Therefore, we have spared no effort to establish such departments. Also, Chinese people are inherently fond of going to lively places, such as the Northeast and the border regions. There are many businesses to be done there, but no one cares about them. This is the purpose of the establishment of these departments. Other departments such as municipal administration, accounting, and education are also important. Therefore, we have paid special attention to the enrollment of specialized departments recently. In other words, the most important criterion for admission is the applicant's ideology.

Zhengfeng College of Arts Enhances Content

Zhengfeng College of Arts, located at No. 1 Jiaozhou Road in Shanghai, has purchased more than ten mu of land opposite Zhongshan Road at the intersection of Jiaotong Road this year and is actively preparing to build school buildings. As there has been a shortage of talent in history and geography, the school has been searching for history and geography professors from various schools, but it has been difficult to find suitable people. Therefore, it has added a Department of History and Geography and hired Chen Yixian, the former editor of the Editorial Office of the Ministry of Education in Beijing, as the department head. Mr. Chen has years of experience in reviewing history and geography textbooks and has served as a professor at various universities in Peiping. He has rich knowledge and experience. Zhou Jinglian, a history graduate of the Central University, has also been hired to teach history courses. After the new school building on Jiaotong Road is completed, a Department of Language and Writing will be added, focusing on Mongolian and Tibetan languages, in order to prepare for the development of the Northwest and train specialists in this field.

Rotary Cup

International Tennis Quarter-Finals, Day One 172

China Wins Two Singles Matches Against the United States 173

Portugal and Japan Each Win One Set

|Doubles Matches, a Total of Two Sets, This Afternoon|

The Shanghai International Tennis Rotary Cup quarter-finals began yesterday at the China Tennis Club. Two to three hundred spectators were present. The matches were between China and the United States, and Japan and Portugal, a total of four singles matches. The battle between China and the United States was one-sided, with both sets won by China. The matches between Japan and Portugal were evenly matched, with each winning one singles set. Machida of Japan played a dramatic five-set match against H. Corassa of Portugal, before the winner was decided. Machida lost due to exhaustion. Today will be the doubles matches, with Japan vs. Portugal starting at 3:00 PM and China vs. the United States starting at 4:30 PM. The location is still at the China Tennis Club. Details are recorded below:

▲China Wins Two Against the United States▲

▲Zheng Zhaojia Wins Against Skuyar 174

This set started at 3:00 PM. Little Zheng won the first and second sets quite easily, both with scores of 6-1. Skuyar's serves often resulted in double faults, reducing his original power. Zheng Zhaojia, on the other hand, was full of energy, able to reduce errors, and used his intelligence to win. Combined with strong smashes, he showed that his tennis skills have made considerable progress. However, Zheng surprisingly lost the third set with a score of 1-6, which is truly strange, reducing the audience's confidence. Perhaps Zheng thought victory was guaranteed, and deliberately prolonged the match to satisfy his "tennis desire"? The fourth set was completed in one go with five games, and in the fifth game, Zheng was serving, and was initially down 0-40, but then won five consecutive points to recapture the game, which was not easy. In the sixth game, Zheng deliberately hit the ball into the net, giving away a game. However, Skuyar then won the next two games, finally ending the set 6-3.

At the end of the five sets, Corassa still showed no signs of fatigue. Corassa was able to save the ball regardless of whether it was short or long distance, but his control was still lacking, with many balls hitting the net or going out of bounds. Machida won the first and third sets, but in the fourth set, Corassa won 6-1. In the fifth set, after Machida took the first game, he lost six consecutive games. Essays

Too Much and Too Little Courage 182

— Pei Yu

"Excess and deficiency" are not good, "too much" and "too little" are not good. Which is worse, "excess" and "too much," or "deficiency" and "too little?" That is difficult to determine. Most people always think this way: "deficiency" and "too little" are comparatively worse.

This view cannot be praised! Too little courage! This is the cry of many among us. Mr. Zhang San wants to be an artist, but his father opposes it and forces him to be an engineer. If he fails as an engineer, he will have the self-deprecating self-comfort of "if I had been an artist, I would definitely have soared." Miss Li Si wants to be a singer and dancer, but is prevented by her family and cannot fulfill her wish, resulting in the burial of her talent. In this situation, it is indeed "too little" that is comparatively worse.

In fact, "too much" is not necessarily less bad, especially in terms of courage. Too much courage easily destroys inherent aspirations completely. The harm of "too much" is many times greater than the harm of "too little"! Others did not dare to harm Yue Fei, but Qin Hui dared greatly and especially. Others did not want to declare themselves emperors, but Yuan Shikai had a great courage. Others did not have the courage to sign treaties that lost power and humiliated the country, but Li Hongzhang had so much courage that it could not be suppressed. In this situation, it is indeed "too much" that is comparatively worse.

Resisting violent enemies, charging into battle, this kind of courage, only worry about it being "too little," not worry about it being "too much." Enduring humiliation and not being willing to strive forward, this kind of courage only worry about it being "too much," not worry about it being "too little." Therefore, in matters of national importance, please, the courage of those in power, rather than "too much," is better "too little." Too little courage, at most, gives people a scolding of "holding a position and doing nothing." Too much courage inevitably leads to the bad name of "leaving a stink for ten thousand years."

If you want to say a truly accurate word, it should be like this: to do great things that benefit the country and the people, courage should be "too much"; to do deeds that harm the country and the people, courage should be "too little." This is the motto for officials.

Recording Notes 183

— Wang Ruoqi

My old friend Wen Junyehe, since he left the journalist life of the press world in the 15th year of the Republic of China and entered the education world, the literary world in Shanghai has not seen his works for a long time. Except for a small number of new and old friends who have a good relationship with Jun, people are probably very few who know his whereabouts in recent years! In fact, in the past few years, he has been going south to Baiyue and north to Pingjin. In addition to teaching students with blackboards and chalk, he is still diligently studying. He is a scholar with a desire for knowledge like Mr. Liang Xinhui, so if there is something unknown in a certain area of ​​Chinese literature, there is nothing he will not exhaust the origins of in order to fully understand it before he is finished. He originally liked to study ancient literature such as phonology and tortoise shells. Recently, he has also studied local linguistics related to phonology. A few days ago, he suddenly wrote me a letter asking me to introduce him to recording. I thought my old friend didn't like music and opera, so why would he want to record at this moment? Later, I made an appointment and invited him to my residence, and then went together. In addition to Jun, there was also a Mr. Kong who came that day, who is said to be Jun's high achiever. (He is the author of the "What to do" collection) There was also a Mr. Yun. After a chat, I learned that the sound Jun wanted to record was many Siamese letters used in the Siamese language. This Mr. Yun is Siamese, and Junyehe will have to go to Beiping to teach soon, and the sounds of those Siamese letters are very difficult to remember, so he asked Mr. Yun to specially record the pronunciation of the letters on a record for his research materials in the future. Jun's rich research spirit can be seen from this, so I recorded it above.

From Waiting for Employment to "Oppression" 184

— Liuxing

As long as we pay a little attention when stepping on the road, we can see many maids and elder sisters sitting densely in the "recommendation shops" waiting for employment. These are all people who have been exiled from the abandoned countryside. The labor they spend in the countryside cannot even support themselves, so they have to throw themselves into this big city and use their labor to exchange a bowl of rice to eat in wealthy people's homes.

We can imagine what kind of people wealthy people regard maids as. They have to get up earlier than their masters and have to sleep later than their masters. If they do something that the masters are not satisfied with, they will not only be arbitrarily scolded by the masters, but also lose their position of four or five yuan a month. This is still small about their own lives, but the hunger of their parents, in-laws, children, and even unemployed husbands really makes them unable to solve it in any way.

They are helpless people wandering in the metropolis. If they are young and beautiful, they will also be ravaged by the masters and bullied by the male servants. Don't think this is a common thing in the city. This is exactly the morbidity of society.

In the past year, the new films of the Star Company have mostly been picking on a certain morbidity of society and exposing and indicating it. Therefore, one of the above-mentioned social morbidities has also been captured on camera. That is "Oppression," which was first screened at the Central Grand Theater these days.

In "Oppression," we can not only see a tearful story, but its depiction of the destruction of the rural economy can also make people deeply feel the pain. What kind of efforts shall we make to revive our countryside and to relieve the hungry rural men and women in the upside-down situation!

I Also Talk About Qingdao's Bathing Beaches 185

— Bamboo Shadow from Qingdao

Qingdao has four bathing beaches: ㈠ Huiquan, ㈡ West of the Zhanqiao Pier, ㈢ Zhan Mountain, ㈣ Chuanqu Port, etc., but none have the complete facilities of Huiquan.

If you are looking for a place close by, try bathing at the beach near your residence.

If you are looking for a crowded and lively place, a wide beach, clear water, fine sand, and calm tides, then go to Huiquan.

The Huiquan bathing beach has changing rooms, a swimming platform, a music pavilion, rescue boats, water police in yellow uniforms maintaining order, beautiful female bathers like flowers and jade, and waves of fragrant aromas... how orderly and sensual!

If you are not content in your heart and dislike loneliness, then bring a phonograph and a few bottles of soda. Lie on the soft, golden sand, flirt with your lover, turn on the phonograph to play sweet songs, drink your soda, listen to the clanging music, look at the clear blue sea, face your beautiful companion, and sit on the open beach. Wouldn't you feel as if you were in heaven on earth?

Qingdao, praised by everyone as a paradise, Qingdao, the world's park, Qingdao, without severe cold in winter and without extreme heat in summer, out-of-town tourists, why not come?

Under the green shade of trees, on Zhongshan Road, every afternoon, people ride bicycles, drive motorcycles, take rickshaws, or drive new-style small cars, with inflatable rings on their arms, all heading to Huiquan bathing beach for a swim.

The busiest time at the bathing beach is on Sundays and Saturday evenings. If you haven't been there, I guarantee you'll dare to go down. Misses, madams, young mistresses, hair ornaments sparkling, jade bodies lying horizontally, but just take off your clothes and go down. This is a public bathing beach, and no one will interfere, but you must wear a bathing suit.

If you are not good at swimming, be sure to bring an inflatable ring. The inflatable ring, floating in the water and held under your arm, can teach you to advance and retreat freely, and come and go as you please, otherwise you will be left sighing at the vastness of the sea.

Seawater is salty and can cure all kinds of skin diseases, so many tourists come from afar, climbing mountains and sailing seas to try bathing.

The bathing beach is open from July 15th to August 31st every year. The Jiaoji Railway sells discounted round-trip tickets for bathing guests.

Every August, a grand sea祭祀 ceremony is also held, with high platforms erected and fireworks set off, which is especially lively and grand.

When you come to bathe, you don't need to bring a tent, nor do you need to have your lover hold a parasol, because the purpose of sea bathing is to be晒 by the sunlight. Sunlight晒 is very beneficial to your body's health.

You don't need to bring a涼席 or blanket, because there is beautiful, fine sand here that won't soil your玉體 or clothes.

Small Crafts

Simple Homemade Dyes 187

— Bingyu

When chemical industries were not yet developed, purely primitive plant-based dyes were used, which involved boiling the flowers, fruits, peels, and roots of plants to extract various colors for dyeing. Now that chemical industries have advanced, almost all dyes are chemical-based, and the methods for using plant-based dyes are almost lost. However, plant-based dyes are actually more elegant and refined than chemical dyes, and they don't fade. Therefore, in recent years, there has been a revival of promoting primitive plant-based dyes. Now, I will briefly describe the colors that can be obtained from various plants and the dyeing methods.

Generally, when using plant materials such as the flowers, peels, roots, and fruits of草木 to dye fabrics, although the procedures are relatively complex, the elegance of the dyeing and its resistance to sunlight and washing are ultimately unmatched by chemical dyes. However, the colors dyed vary depending on the type of 草木. The most common examples include ㈠ madder roots, safflower flowers,蘇梗 stems, plum branches,丹皮, etc., whose juices extracted by boiling in water can be used to dye red. ㈡刈安草, Huangbo tree bark, gardenia fruit, turmeric root,柿子 seeds, etc., whose juices extracted by boiling in water can be used to dye yellow. ㈢ Hazelnut fruit peels, walnut fruit peels, chestnut fruit peels, bayberry tree bark,亚仙 and coffee seeds,矢車 fruits, black tea, etc., whose juices extracted by boiling in water can be used to dye茶色. ㈣ Blue tree bark,蓬 and pear tree bark, etc., can be used to dye青色. ㈤ Lithospermum roots, 五倍子, etc., can be used to dye purple. ㈥五倍子, chestnut flowers, mulberry wood, black beans, mountain cherry tree bark, etc., can be used to dye mouse gray. ㈦紺藍, lacquer tree leaves, oak tender leaves,矢車 fruits, can be used to dye black. However, these dyes should not be used alone and are often mixed with mordants for better color uptake.

The raw materials for mordants are alum, lye, lime, iron. 重克羅姆酸, aluminum (a soft, light white metal), chromium, tin, rice straw ash, etc. The dyeing method varies depending on what is being dyed. For example, when dyeing cloth and leather, it is necessary to first soak them in the mordant for a whole day and night, then take them out, rinse them clean with water, and soak them in an alkaline solution (i.e., a base dissolved in water) to prevent the mordant from falling off. Then, put them into the dye. If you want to print patterns, after soaking in the mordant, apply wax on top and then immerse it in the dye. In that case, the dye will be transformed into various colors due to the action of the fixed mordant. The most important thing to note here is that the mordant should be thoroughly浸透 and thoroughly washed clean after浸透. In this way, the dye will not run. After soaking in the dye for about ten minutes, dissolve soap in boiling water to melt away the wax, at which point the color will be fixed and will not change. If we want to distinguish the shades of the same color, we need to differentiate based on the type of mordant. If we use it cleverly, it will reveal very attractive colors. For example, alum produces the brightest color, while iron produces a deep, dark color. If we use a decoction of coffee beans to dye, we can first use alum as a mordant to turn it into a light tea color, then use lime as a mordant to turn it into a slightly darker茶色. If we then use a copper sulfate solution as a mordant, it will turn into a gray-tinted茶色. Finally, when iron is used as a mordant, it will turn into a black-tinted茶色, thus becoming the color of coffee. Therefore, according to the pattern, the wax left on the color gradually separates into shades of concentration within the same color due to the use of mordant procedures. Although this dyeing method is cumbersome, the colors dyed are more unique than those dyed with chemical dyes. As for the dyeing utensils, it is advisable to use pottery. When dyeing leather, tannin or chromium can be used, which will not fade even after prolonged exposure to sunlight. When using other rose flowers as a dye, Aniline black naphthalene solution can be used to soak white rose flowers with stems, which will turn gray or light black. The most suitable dye mixture is one-eighth of an ounce of dye mixed with three合 two勺 of water.

Causes and Cures for Weak Sound in AC Radios 190

— One Who Knows

An AC radio, when bought or assembled, often has a loud and clear tone, which is very satisfactory. However, after using it for a period of time, the tone will gradually become weaker. The reasons for this are approximately as follows:

㈠ Due to the vacuum tube, after long-term use, the efficiency of electron emission is greatly reduced. The electron tube is the soul of the radio, like the brain in the human body. If the main brain loses its sensitive perception, the receiving efficiency will naturally be greatly reduced. When encountering this problem, you can only replace the electron tube with a new one or apply the resurrection method. Also, if the electron tube is used continuously for too long, it will generate high heat, and the emission of electrons inside the tube will exceed the specified range, and the receiving efficiency will also be reduced. When encountering this problem, you should quickly stop using the machine and restart it after the electron tube has cooled down.

㈡ Due to the transformer, if the high-power transformer is used continuously, both the copper wires and the iron sheets will generate high heat, thus increasing the resistance of the copper wires and the magnetic resistance of the iron sheets. If the eddy current loss (EDDY CURRENT LOSS) and the hysteresis loss (HYSTERESIS LOSS) on the iron sheet greatly increase, then the transformer will suffer a great invisible consumption, resulting in a great reduction in the output load power. If the radio has insufficient power, how can it have excellent reception?

㈢ Due to the capacitor, if the electrolytic filter or the capacitor with poor insulation is used for a long time, dust will accumulate, and in humid weather, it will easily cause part of the power to cross over, thus, the required voltage will lose a part, and the power will feel insufficient, and the sound will naturally be weakened.

㈣ Due to the resistor, carbon resistors cannot withstand high temperatures. If they are used for too long, the temperature will increase continuously, and the resistance will also continue to increase continuously. If the resistance is large, the current passing through will be small, and the electron tube will not get the appropriate current, and the receiving efficiency will be greatly reduced.

㈤ Due to the volume control, the volume control (VOLUMEGRAD) is made by coating carbon powder on an insulator to form a circle and adjusting it with a movable lever. Sometimes, after long-term use, the carbon powder decreases due to friction, the resistance increases, and the sound becomes weak.

㈥ Due to the wiring, improper wiring and loosening over time will reduce the contact area between the two conductors, increase the resistance, and the radio will also become weak.

In summary, the reasons for the weak sound of AC radios are due to: ㈠ continued use for too long, vacuum tubes, transformers, and resistors exceed their specified temperatures and lose their effectiveness; ㈡ dust accumulation and moisture intrusion cause leakage; ㈢ poor construction of the machine parts. Therefore, we should pay attention when using it: ㈠ Do not leave it on for too long. It is best to turn it off for two or three minutes after using it for one or two hours; ㈡ Do not place it in a humid place, and do not let dust get in. After a few months, blow away the accumulated dust inside; ㈢ Do not be greedy for temporary cheapness and buy inferior goods for each machine part, otherwise, you will lose more than you gain in the future. Pay attention to the wiring and use tin solder to fix it firmly, which can be done once and for all.

An Improved Regeneration Circuit 191

— Shi Huayu

When we design a shortwave machine, the most difficult thing is that the oscillation caused by ordinary regeneration coils cannot be very stable. We now discard the regeneration coil and use the circuit in the attached figure. Then we can get good results. This circuit only uses one plug-in coil L, so changing the wavelength is very convenient, and it can be applied from tens of meters to the broadcast wavelength band. In the figure, the grid and screen of the tube are coupled using the primary of the headphones or the low-frequency transformer. Therefore, the regenerative force is not generated by the ordinary regeneration coil or variable capacitor, but by the resistance. In addition, the antenna is coupled by a capacitor as in the ordinary method, but C2 has two functions: one, the regenerative force can occur within a very wide adjustment range, and two, the adjustment circuit only has self-inductance. In short, the advantage of this circuit is that it can receive various wavelengths with only a coil change.

Adjustment and Steps of a Shortwave Transmitter (Continued) 192

— Luo Jingyu

The above chapter on the principle and steps of single-oscillation adjustment

The Chinese translation of single-oscillation is also called self-made type, including three main circuits: Hartley, TPTG (TUNED PLATE GRID), and Colpitts. According to the method of matching, it is divided into two categories: inductive coupling (LNDUCTIVE COUPLING) and capacitive coupling (CAPACITVE COUPLING). However, although the method of matching has such categories, the purpose is the same, which is to return the plate current to the grid and ask him to oscillate.

If the steps for single-oscillation adjustment are described in detail, there will naturally be many, but the general division can be divided into the following five stages:

㈠ If we have constructed all the equipment according to a certain established circuit (the three main circuits will be discussed in detail in paragraph (3)), then the first point we need to check is whether the positions of the various installations are appropriate, the second point is whether the various wirings are firm and reliable, and the third point is whether the coil used matches the wavelength we expected. Secondly,

㈡ Light the filament to the rated voltage. If it is in a colder season, it is best to let the filament burn alone for a minute or two to make its heat sufficient, and then add the plate voltage. (This situation is especially emphasized in old-fashioned鐺製 vacuum tubes: because this type of vacuum tube will not have electrons flying out of the filament unless it reaches the highest heat.) The filament voltage can sometimes be slightly changed during the adjustment process: but if it is too high, the vacuum tube will be easily damaged, and if it is too low, it will not easily oscillate. As for the plate voltage, it can usually be half of the rated value during adjustment, or even as high as two-thirds weak. For example, we mostly use 50-watt vacuum tubes up to 500 or 600 volts. A 250-watt vacuum tube can be used up to 1,000 or 1,200 volts. Then

㈢ Re-tune the oscillation circuit. The method is to first remove the antenna, or make the antenna coil very loosely coupled, and then start the tuning work of the oscillation circuit. Also, because there are differences between inductive coupling and capacitive coupling, the procedures for tuning the oscillation circuit are also different. I will now describe them separately below. However, before starting the description, we have to understand that the quality of the tuning oscillation also determines the efficiency of the machine itself. As mentioned earlier, a good oscillation situation is to minimize the plate current: therefore, when we change the number of turns of the coil up and down (such as Hartley) or move the number of degrees of the capacitor (such as Colpitts, etc.), when we stop at a certain point, the positions on both sides are based on increasing the number of plate currents: then the certain point where the machine stops is the standard point for the best oscillation situation. Of course, this situation can also be said to indicate the highest point of the machine's own efficiency. (To be continued)

How to Adjust the Lowest Bass (Continued) 193

— Guan Zhibing

What I'm talking about is the tone problem, so let's talk about the tones of these two radio stations: when listening to XCBL, its lowest bass only reaches 蓬!蓬!蓬! and stops there; and it also seems to lack a bit of echo, but when listening to ZMHY, below 蓬!蓬!蓬! you can still hear the tone of 洪!洪!洪!, and below this tone of 洪!洪!洪! there is an unlimited spare volume, as if standing on a high mountain and looking down at a deep abyss, wanting it to be high, it goes straight up to the blue sky, wanting it to be low, it sinks into the unfathomable abyss.

Now let's get back to the topic and talk about how the lowest bass is cut off. How can the lowest bass be adjusted? As mentioned in the previous section, the quality of the tone depends entirely on the low-frequency amplifier, which is beyond doubt. However, even with the same machine, slightly changing its adjustment can cut off or obtain the possibility of the lowest bass. It seems that more attention needs to be paid to the adjustment. According to the author's speculation, generally, those who make adjustments often feel that the tone is not loud enough, so they focus on the last two stages of low-frequency amplification or perhaps add two stages of amplification. If they feel that it is too loud, the control is mostly in the last two stages, or the controller at the pickup stage is used to control it. In this way, the high-frequency part is amplified and the low-frequency part is cut off without being aware of it.

Experience tells me that if you want to adjust the lowest bass, you must

Amplify the first two stages of the low-frequency amplifier as much as possible, paying special attention to the pickup stage, so that the original sound is emitted as faithfully as possible, but it should not be amplified too much to cause distortion, or it will cut off the highest treble.

I have now drawn the circuit diagram of my machine above. When A is amplified as much as possible and B is reduced, the lowest bass can be obtained, but on the contrary, if B is amplified and A is reduced, the lowest bass will be cut off and unheard. Therefore, I think that the low-frequency amplifier must amplify the first two stages as much as possible and not increase the consumption resistance, resulting in the cutting off of its lowest bass.

I wrote the above text specifically for the reference of fellow radio researchers, and I hope that you will supplement or correct it after the experiment, that would be even better. (End)

Fuses for Radio 194

— Ke Ming

A new type of "LITTLEFUSES" has recently come onto the American market that can be used in various radio circuits. Its current carrying capacity ranges from ten milliamperes to two amperes, with different low and high voltages.

Low-voltage small fuses are shaped like glass tube-style grid leak resistors and are ideal for protecting various AC and DC milliampere meters, low-voltage ammeters, voltmeters, etc. The installation methods include using grid leak resistor brackets or using clips that can be connected to flexible wires, as well as the plug-in method used for lightning protection devices, which requires adding corresponding insertion materials.

High-voltage fuses have several types such as one thousand, five thousand, and ten thousand volts, with lengths ranging from three inches to ten inches to suit various high-voltage fusing amounts. The fuse holder is made of porcelain or a clip with a base with considerable insulation. This high-voltage fuse is used to protect the rectifier tube and the transmitting tube from overload.

Common Sense 196

— Huang Jiancun

(13) Tuning Circuit

(1) The Meaning of Tuning: To understand the function of a tuning circuit, one must first understand what tuning is and its unique characteristics. Here is a diagram to illustrate its meaning: Figure 1 shows a circuit composed of a capacitor C, an inductor L, and a resistor R. If an alternating current (AC) power source is connected to this circuit, current will circulate back and forth within it. If the frequency of the AC power source is varied one by one until it reaches an appropriate frequency, the current flowing through the circuit will be at its maximum. This phenomenon is called tuning, and the frequency possessed by the power source at this time is called the tuning frequency. If the frequency of the power source remains constant, and the capacitance C or inductance L in the circuit is increased or decreased, the point where the current is at its maximum can also be adjusted. This phenomenon also belongs to tuning.

(2) Relationship between Tuning Frequency and CL: Let F be the tuning frequency, with its unit in kilocycles (KC); C be the capacitance, with its unit in microfarads (MF); L be the inductance, with its unit in microhenries (MH); when there is the following relationship between F and CL, the tuning phenomenon occurs.

And its tuning wavelength (in meters) is:

(3) Tuning Circuit of a Radio: The tuning circuit of a radio is composed of a capacitor and an inductor, and it is the main gateway of the radio. All incoming radio waves must pass through this gateway. By varying the capacitance of the capacitor one by one, one can select the incoming wavelengths to be received. The range of the tuning wavelength is determined by the combination of capacitance and inductance. Currently, the wavelength range used for broadcasting is from 200 meters to 545 meters. Therefore, to suit this wavelength range, the number of plates of the variable capacitor and the number of turns of the inductor should be appropriately selected. The method of selection will be described in detail in another article.

Before measuring a capacitor, you must first try to verify that the capacitor is not damaged or short-circuited. Otherwise, there is a risk of burning out the meter and fuse. This point should be especially noted.

Small Experience

Method for Cutting Gramophone Records 197

— Hu Jingyong

Using discarded gramophone records to make the front and back panels of smaller radios is no different in function from bakelite boards. However, sawing them into the appropriate size to meet the needs is more difficult than sawing bakelite boards because they are thin and brittle and easily broken if not handled carefully. Therefore, those who want to use them often encounter difficulties. I will now record the two cutting methods I use. If you follow these methods, you will surely be satisfied.

Place the gramophone record and use a soapstone pencil and a metal ruler to draw the desired size. Then, use a small paper cutter to draw a groove along the drawn line, with a depth of about half the thickness of the record. Then align the groove with the edge of the table and lightly press down with your hand, and it will break easily.

The method of drawing the size is the same as before. Then place the record on a flat board, prepare a wooden strip, and place a flat-edged kitchen knife on the stove fire. When the knife is slightly red, press the wooden strip on the soapstone pencil line drawn on the record surface and cut it flat with the knife, just like cutting a cake, without any effort. However, the former method is superior to the latter because the edge of the record is smoother.
